Content: Dental Insurance & Finances | Dolphin Dental | East York Toronto Dentist (416) 429-3317 Book Now (416) 429-3317 dolphingenie@rogers.com Why Choose Dolphin Dental Dental Insurance & Finances Dental Appointment & Office Policies FAQs Health & Safety Services Family Dentistry Children’s Dentistry Happy Visits Cavity Free Club Fillings and Extractions Sports Mouthguards Early Intervention Orthodontics Emergency Dentistry Dental Hygiene & Teeth Cleanings Root Canal Therapy Clear Aligners Orthodontics TMJ/TMD Therapy Bruxism Grinding Appliances Clear Aligners Cosmetic Dentistry Teeth Whitening Dental Crowns Dental Bridges Porcelain Veneers Cosmetic Tooth Bonding Dental Implants White Fillings Porcelain Inlays & Onlays Oral Surgery Tooth Extractions Wisdom Teeth Extractions Dental Implants Periodontal Care Gum Disease Oral Health Laser Dental Treatment New Patients Team Dr. Priya Rao Dental Assistant Team Dental Hygienists Team Dental Administration Team Contact Book Now Dental Insurance & Finances Dentist Dental Insurance Dental Insurance At Dolphin Dental, we are committed to providing our patients with personalized, high-quality dental services at affordable prices, and we follow the most up-to-date Ontario Fee Guide for all our dental services. We understand that Dental Insurance & Finances can be confusing and paying for dental treatment can be stressful, especially if the costs are high. You should consider yourself fortunate if you have insurance benefits to help with the cost of your dental care. Please know that our goal is to assist you in navigating your coverage so that you obtain the maximum benefits possible. Dolphin Dental is here to assist you in understanding your insurance plan so you can best utilize your coverage. To guarantee accuracy when dealing with your insurance company, please bring your most up-to-date insurance information with you to your appointment. Dental insurance is a complex subject; while it is not possible for us to know every detail, limit, or exclusion involved in all the plans we deal with, we endeavor to assist you in understanding and navigating coverage details the very best we can. Our office prides itself on providing a very high standard of dental care at a very fair price. Please know that dental insurance is intended to cover some, but not all, of the costs of your dental care. Not all dental plans are the same, and not all treatments are eligible or fully reimbursable. Furthermore, insurance companies can sometimes make it difficult for the dental provider to retrieve any extended information. It is, therefore, important to remember that it is ultimately your responsibility to understand what your individual plan allows. Please note that the treatment we recommend will always be based on your dental needs, regardless of the nature and extent of your dental plan coverage. We Offer Direct Insurance Billing! Direct Billing We are pleased to offer Direct Billing (also called “Assignment of Benefits”). Our administrative team is happy to electronically submit your insurance papers directly to your insurance company on your behalf and accept their payment directly to our office. You only pay the difference your company will not cover. Unfortunately, there are a few insurance companies that will not allow payment to come to the office, therefore payment in full for services is required. Please note that despite our efforts, due to the Canadian Personal Privacy Act, we have limited access to any specific information from your dental insurance company regarding your plan. It is your responsibility to know the parameters of your dental coverage plan and to provide our office with accurate and current insurance information. Insurance We accept most major insurance providers. Please call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 if you have any inquiries regarding our insurance partners. Payment We offer several payment options for your convenience, including Cash, Debit Card, Visa, and MasterCard. If you have any questions about your dental insurance please do not hesitate to call us at (416) 429-3317 , or email us at dolphingenie@rogers.com . We look forward to hearing from you soon. Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up an appointment today! In order to ensure that your next dental appointment is as pleasant and predictable as possible, we would like to give you an overview of our office policies. Please feel free to call us at (416) 429-3317 with any questions you may have. Your East York Choice for All Your Dental Needs! Reasons Please understand that it is ultimately your responsibility to keep track of any upcoming dental appointment. As a courtesy, we send out hygiene reminders a few weeks before a requested appointment, and we make confirmation calls or emails two weeks before hygiene appointments. As well, we send a courtesy reminder the day before all appointments . Although we make every effort to contact you before any appointment, it is ultimately your responsibility to ensure that you will be at your appointment unless other arrangements have been made in advance with our office. Due to a continuous high demand for prime appointment times, we require a minimum of 2 business days’ notice per appointment should you need to reschedule or cancel your appointment. Because we value your time, we do not double book our clients. As such, your appointment is a valuable time that the doctor has set aside, especially for you. Where insufficient notice is given, a missed appointment fee may be charged to you, or we may require you to prepay to reserve your next appointment. Our goal is always to provide you with a pleasant experience. We strive to serve you to the very best of our ability, and we are committed to helping you attain the highest level of dental and overall well-being. If you have any questions about any of our policies or procedures, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 , or email us at dolphingenie@rogers.com We look forward to hearing from you soon. Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up an appointment today! Content: FAQs | Dolphin Dental | East York Toronto Family Dentist | 416-429-3317 (416) 429-3317 Book Now (416) 429-3317 dolphingenie@rogers.com Why Choose Dolphin Dental Dental Insurance & Finances Dental Appointment & Office Policies FAQs Health & Safety Services Family Dentistry Children’s Dentistry Happy Visits Cavity Free Club Fillings and Extractions Sports Mouthguards Early Intervention Orthodontics Emergency Dentistry Dental Hygiene & Teeth Cleanings Root Canal Therapy Clear Aligners Orthodontics TMJ/TMD Therapy Bruxism Grinding Appliances Clear Aligners Cosmetic Dentistry Teeth Whitening Dental Crowns Dental Bridges Porcelain Veneers Cosmetic Tooth Bonding Dental Implants White Fillings Porcelain Inlays & Onlays Oral Surgery Tooth Extractions Wisdom Teeth Extractions Dental Implants Periodontal Care Gum Disease Oral Health Laser Dental Treatment New Patients Team Dr. Priya Rao Dental Assistant Team Dental Hygienists Team Dental Administration Team Contact Book Now Frequently Asked Questions (FAQs) Dentist Have Questions? We Have Answers! FAQs Dolphin Dental is always here to address all your oral health needs. We believe that each and every patient deserves personalized attention and care, with the goal of creating a lifetime of beautiful and healthy smiles. We are often asked questions, and it is always our goal to answer them. Below are some FAQs  (frequently asked questions) to help you learn more about Dolphin Dental. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. Does Dolphin Dental direct bill insurance companies? Yes! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer direct insurance billing , as long as your plan allows it. Do you follow the current Ontario Dental Association Fee Guide? Yes. Dolphin Dental follows the recommended Ontario Dental Association Ontario Dental Fee Guide for all procedure codes. Do you offer evening and weekend appointments? Yes. For your convenience, Dolphin Dental is open until 7pm Monday-Friday, and Saturdays 10:00-4:00. When should I bring my child in for their first visit? Dolphin Dental recommends that you bring your child in within 6 months of the eruption of their first tooth, or by the age of one, whichever comes first. Do you have payment plans? At this time, Dolphin Dental does not have payment plans available. However, we will do our best to work around your budget. Do you perform wisdom teeth extractions at your office? Yes. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer wisdom teeth extractions . We will need to first examine and take a panoramic x-ray to determine if you are a good candidate to have them removed here. If we are unable to perform the procedure in office we will refer you to a very caring specialists in the neighbourhood Do you offer teeth whitening? Can I bill it to my insurance? Yes! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer two different teeth whitening options. In-house teeth whitening for faster results, or take-home teeth whitening trays you can do in the privacy and convenience of your own home. Unfortunately, dental insurance does not cover cosmetic bleaching. Do you offer emergency appointments? Absolutely! Dolphin Dental will do everything we can to see you the same day. Please call us at (416) 429-3317 if you are having a dental emergency. Do you offer Clear Aligners? Yes, Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer Clear Aligners at our office. Your dentist will determine if you are a good candidate for this treatment. My teeth feel fine, do I still need to come in for a check-up? Yes. Dolphin Dental recommends that you come in regularly to ensure we prevent or catch common dental problems early on, such as gum disease and tooth decay from forming. I’m pregnant/breastfeeding. Can I still come to my appointment? Yes. Dolphin Dental recommends dental cleanings for pregnant women at 12 and 24 weeks. X-Rays will not be taken unless there is an urgent issue. If you are breastfeeding, please continue to see the dentist/hygienist for your regular preventative care. How often should I come in for a check-up/cleaning? This depends on the condition of your mouth. It could range anywhere from every 3 months to every 9 months. On average, we typically see patients once every 6 months. Your dentist will determine what schedule is best for you, based on your circumstances. What is a dental crown? A dental crown is a covering or ‘cap’ for your damaged tooth. It restores your tooth to its normal shape, size, and function. It is typically recommended for a structurally weak tooth that is at high risk of breaking. Do you do dental implants at your office? Yes. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer dental implants . We will start with a consultation to determine if you are a good candidate. Do Root Canals/Fillings hurt? During your root canal, we will use a local anesthetic to keep you as comfortable as possible during the procedure. Afterwards, some soreness is normal and can be managed using over the counter pain killers/analgesics. Can I get x-rays with metal braces? Yes. It is completely safe to have x-rays taken on your teeth during your active orthodontic treatment. It is imperative to regularly come in with braces as they can be a bit tricky to clean! Can you tell me what my plan covers? As a courtesy, we try our best to verify all codes prior to you coming in to avoid any surprises! Some plans have services available to dental providers to verify your coverage. Unfortunately, some other providers have very strict privacy rules where they will only release this information to the subscriber of the plan, not the dental office. This means it is not always possible for us to verify on your behalf. Why does my insurance plan only cover an exam every 9 months but, my dentist wants me to come every 6? A dentist’s first priority is your health. Your dentist will first present a plan based on your oral health needs, which may or may not be covered by your dental plan. Your dentist can do their best to work within your plan whenever possible. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. We look forward to hearing from you soon. Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up an appointment today! At Dolphin Dental, we are committed to your health and safety at all times. We take our sterilization and infection control procedures very seriously to ensure that your dental health and safety are protected at all times. In light of the current COVID-19 outbreak, we understand that many of our patients have questions about our safety practices. Please know that we are taking all precautions to ensure our staff and patient’s safety, and we follow very strict sterilization and infection control procedures in our office. Our Health and Safety Measures Clean Clinic & Equipment OHS Screening of all patients & staff before entering the clinic Sneezeguards have been installed at reception. Constant hand sanitizing of all patients and staff upon initial entry/exit of the office, with hand sanitizer positioned throughout the clinic Enhanced and frequent disinfection of all contact surfaces All magazines/toys and items that can harbour or transfer germs have been removed from the waiting room. All patients, accompanying adults, and team members wear masks at all times when inside the practice. We are happy to provide you with one if you do not have your own. Patients are asked to limit companions at their appointments. Accompanying individuals are asked to wait in the mall or in their vehicles (exception being a legal guardian). Enhanced Complete Personal Protective Equipment (PPE) that follows recommended guidelines from Ontario Health Services and the Ontario Dental Association. Social distancing in clinic Providing teledentistry services – if required for follow-up lab reports or communication that can be done online or through video education Online paperwork that we require from all new patients that can be filled out beforehand (which are mobile and easy) Please be assured that our health and safety plan is thorough and put in place with your health and safety in mind. It will continue to evolve as we continue to learn how to best manage protocol, and this section will be updated regularly and accordingly.  Please feel free to contact us at any time if you have any questions regarding your health and safety or any of our health and safety procedures. If you have any questions about any of these policies, please do not hesitate to call us at (416) 429-3317 , or email us at dolphingenie@rogers.ca . We look forward to hearing from you soon. Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up an appointment today! Content: Children's Dentistry | Dolphin Dental | East York Dentist | 416-429-3317 (416) 429-3317 Book Now (416) 429-3317 dolphingenie@rogers.com Why Choose Dolphin Dental Dental Insurance & Finances Dental Appointment & Office Policies FAQs Health & Safety Services Family Dentistry Children’s Dentistry Happy Visits Cavity Free Club Fillings and Extractions Sports Mouthguards Early Intervention Orthodontics Emergency Dentistry Dental Hygiene & Teeth Cleanings Root Canal Therapy Clear Aligners Orthodontics TMJ/TMD Therapy Bruxism Grinding Appliances Clear Aligners Cosmetic Dentistry Teeth Whitening Dental Crowns Dental Bridges Porcelain Veneers Cosmetic Tooth Bonding Dental Implants White Fillings Porcelain Inlays & Onlays Oral Surgery Tooth Extractions Wisdom Teeth Extractions Dental Implants Periodontal Care Gum Disease Oral Health Laser Dental Treatment New Patients Team Dr. Priya Rao Dental Assistant Team Dental Hygienists Team Dental Administration Team Contact Book Now Children’s Dentistry East York Dentist Your East York Choice for Children’s Dentistry! Children's Dolphin Dental is proud to offer services to patients of ALL ages. We are pleased to offer Children’s Dentistry services tailored specifically to children and their unique needs, from birth all the way to adolescence. Dolphin Dental believes in the importance of creating a positive experience at the dentist early on, in order to encourage a lifetime of good oral care. As parents ourselves, we understand the unique concerns and fears that children often have. With our family-friendly atmosphere, and our caring and always-smiling team members, we are here to make sure your child’s visit to the dentist is a happy one, each and every time. Our goal with pediatric visits is to ensure that your child is always comfortable and relaxed, while also setting the foundation they can draw from for the rest of their life. We hope your child leaves eager and enthusiastic to continue on with their future dental visits! When should I bring my child to the dentist for the first time? Dentistry The Canadian Dental Association recommends that children obtain a dental examination within 6 months of the eruption of their first tooth, or by the age of one, whichever comes first. It is important to see children early on, and review important aspects of dental care, health, and diet. Happy Visits Happy Visits Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer complimentary Happy Visits to all children under the age of 3. We aim to ensure these visits are fun, and that children feel safe and relaxed throughout. Our goal is to introduce your child to the dental visit experience and allow them to become familiar with the entire process, while ensuring it is enjoyable. These visits help ensure that your child has a positive association with the dentist and oral health in general, which will set the stage for a lifetime of good oral health. Cavity Free Club Cavity Free This is a club your kids will want to be a part of! Our cavity-free club acts as a reward system to help our youngest patients learn and maintain good oral hygiene habits. Every young patient may become a member; all they have to do is take care of their teeth by brushing and flossing daily, and if they come to their appointment and have no cavities, they become a member! Once they become a member, they will be entered into a draw to receive a monthly prize. They will also receive a small toy which they can choose from our cavity-free club reward chest! Fillings and Extractions Fillings If your child has a damaged or cracked tooth in need of repair, we may recommend a filling, which will help prevent bacteria from entering the crack or damaged area of the tooth. Fillings in children are just as necessary as they are for adults, because untreated cavities can cause discomfort and pain, and cavities can lead to other problems including infection. Extractions may also be necessary, depending on the health of a tooth, whether there is any overcrowding, or in preparation for orthodontic treatment later on. Our dentists will discuss with you any recommendations regarding fillings and extractions for your child. Rest assured that should your child require a filling or an extraction, they will remain pain-free, comfortable, and relaxed throughout the entire procedure. For more complicated procedures your child may be referred to a specialist. Sports Mouthguards Sports If your child has a damaged or cracked tooth in need of repair, we may recommend a filling, which will help prevent bacteria from entering the crack or damaged area of the tooth. Fillings in children are just as necessary as they are for adults, because untreated cavities can cause discomfort and pain, and cavities can lead to other problems including infection. Extractions may also be necessary, depending on the health of a tooth, whether there is any overcrowding, or in preparation for orthodontic treatment later on. Our dentists will discuss with you any recommendations regarding fillings and extractions for your child. Rest assured that should your child require a filling or an extraction, they will remain pain-free, comfortable, and relaxed throughout the entire procedure. For more complicated procedures your child may be referred to a specialist. Early Intervention Orthodontics Orthodontics Early intervention orthodontics is orthodontic treatment for children starting around the age of 7. Intervening early on can reduce the need for tooth extraction and jaw surgery later on, correct certain problems before they appear, encourage better facial development, shorten the length of time of any orthodontic treatment needed later on, and provide patients with a better overall result in the end. Traditional orthodontic treatment begins after most or all of a patient’s adult teeth have grown in. However, certain issues with dental alignment, bite, and facial development can begin to appear long before the last few adult teeth appear. By correcting any of these problems early on, future orthodontic treatment can be faster and easier, and sometimes even unnecessary! It is important to note that not all orthodontic problems can be solved with early intervention, which is why it is important that your child have an initial consultation with their dentist as soon as possible after they turn seven. Dolphin Dental is committed to ensuring children get an early start on their oral journey so that their teeth, gums, and smile are healthy from day one. We are pleased to provide dental care to children of any age, and we take special care to ensure our youngest patients always feel comfortable and safe. If you have any questions about the oral health needs of your child, or you would like to set up a visit for your child, call us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to help! Book Now We look forward to hearing from you soon! Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up your Children’s Dentistry appointment today! Content: Children's Dentistry | Dolphin Dental | East York Dentist | 416-429-3317 (416) 429-3317 Book Now (416) 429-3317 dolphingenie@rogers.com Why Choose Dolphin Dental Dental Insurance & Finances Dental Appointment & Office Policies FAQs Health & Safety Services Family Dentistry Children’s Dentistry Happy Visits Cavity Free Club Fillings and Extractions Sports Mouthguards Early Intervention Orthodontics Emergency Dentistry Dental Hygiene & Teeth Cleanings Root Canal Therapy Clear Aligners Orthodontics TMJ/TMD Therapy Bruxism Grinding Appliances Clear Aligners Cosmetic Dentistry Teeth Whitening Dental Crowns Dental Bridges Porcelain Veneers Cosmetic Tooth Bonding Dental Implants White Fillings Porcelain Inlays & Onlays Oral Surgery Tooth Extractions Wisdom Teeth Extractions Dental Implants Periodontal Care Gum Disease Oral Health Laser Dental Treatment New Patients Team Dr. Priya Rao Dental Assistant Team Dental Hygienists Team Dental Administration Team Contact Book Now Children’s Dentistry East York Dentist Your East York Choice for Children’s Dentistry! Children's Dolphin Dental is proud to offer services to patients of ALL ages. We are pleased to offer Children’s Dentistry services tailored specifically to children and their unique needs, from birth all the way to adolescence. Dolphin Dental believes in the importance of creating a positive experience at the dentist early on, in order to encourage a lifetime of good oral care. As parents ourselves, we understand the unique concerns and fears that children often have. With our family-friendly atmosphere, and our caring and always-smiling team members, we are here to make sure your child’s visit to the dentist is a happy one, each and every time. Our goal with pediatric visits is to ensure that your child is always comfortable and relaxed, while also setting the foundation they can draw from for the rest of their life. We hope your child leaves eager and enthusiastic to continue on with their future dental visits! When should I bring my child to the dentist for the first time? Dentistry The Canadian Dental Association recommends that children obtain a dental examination within 6 months of the eruption of their first tooth, or by the age of one, whichever comes first. It is important to see children early on, and review important aspects of dental care, health, and diet. Happy Visits Happy Visits Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer complimentary Happy Visits to all children under the age of 3. We aim to ensure these visits are fun, and that children feel safe and relaxed throughout. Our goal is to introduce your child to the dental visit experience and allow them to become familiar with the entire process, while ensuring it is enjoyable. These visits help ensure that your child has a positive association with the dentist and oral health in general, which will set the stage for a lifetime of good oral health. Cavity Free Club Cavity Free This is a club your kids will want to be a part of! Our cavity-free club acts as a reward system to help our youngest patients learn and maintain good oral hygiene habits. Every young patient may become a member; all they have to do is take care of their teeth by brushing and flossing daily, and if they come to their appointment and have no cavities, they become a member! Once they become a member, they will be entered into a draw to receive a monthly prize. They will also receive a small toy which they can choose from our cavity-free club reward chest! Fillings and Extractions Fillings If your child has a damaged or cracked tooth in need of repair, we may recommend a filling, which will help prevent bacteria from entering the crack or damaged area of the tooth. Fillings in children are just as necessary as they are for adults, because untreated cavities can cause discomfort and pain, and cavities can lead to other problems including infection. Extractions may also be necessary, depending on the health of a tooth, whether there is any overcrowding, or in preparation for orthodontic treatment later on. Our dentists will discuss with you any recommendations regarding fillings and extractions for your child. Rest assured that should your child require a filling or an extraction, they will remain pain-free, comfortable, and relaxed throughout the entire procedure. For more complicated procedures your child may be referred to a specialist. Sports Mouthguards Sports If your child has a damaged or cracked tooth in need of repair, we may recommend a filling, which will help prevent bacteria from entering the crack or damaged area of the tooth. Fillings in children are just as necessary as they are for adults, because untreated cavities can cause discomfort and pain, and cavities can lead to other problems including infection. Extractions may also be necessary, depending on the health of a tooth, whether there is any overcrowding, or in preparation for orthodontic treatment later on. Our dentists will discuss with you any recommendations regarding fillings and extractions for your child. Rest assured that should your child require a filling or an extraction, they will remain pain-free, comfortable, and relaxed throughout the entire procedure. For more complicated procedures your child may be referred to a specialist. Early Intervention Orthodontics Orthodontics Early intervention orthodontics is orthodontic treatment for children starting around the age of 7. Intervening early on can reduce the need for tooth extraction and jaw surgery later on, correct certain problems before they appear, encourage better facial development, shorten the length of time of any orthodontic treatment needed later on, and provide patients with a better overall result in the end. Traditional orthodontic treatment begins after most or all of a patient’s adult teeth have grown in. However, certain issues with dental alignment, bite, and facial development can begin to appear long before the last few adult teeth appear. By correcting any of these problems early on, future orthodontic treatment can be faster and easier, and sometimes even unnecessary! It is important to note that not all orthodontic problems can be solved with early intervention, which is why it is important that your child have an initial consultation with their dentist as soon as possible after they turn seven. Dolphin Dental is committed to ensuring children get an early start on their oral journey so that their teeth, gums, and smile are healthy from day one. We are pleased to provide dental care to children of any age, and we take special care to ensure our youngest patients always feel comfortable and safe. If you have any questions about the oral health needs of your child, or you would like to set up a visit for your child, call us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to help! Book Now We look forward to hearing from you soon! Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up your Children’s Dentistry appointment today! Emergency At Dolphin Dental, we understand that emergencies sometimes happen! We have seen it all, and we know the importance of dealing with emergency dental issues as soon as possible. If you are unsure whether something is an emergency or not, we offer this advice; if it hurts, it is an emergency! This is because even injuries that seem small or superficial can still affect the living tissue inside of the tooth. When a dental emergency arises, Dolphin Dental is here to help make you smile again. What Constitutes an Emergency? Dentistry Sudden and severe pain that will not go away Swelling and fever A loose tooth A broken, chipped, or cracked tooth A tooth knocked out of its socket Fillings that are causing discomfort or pain, or any dental device malfunction (a retainer, bridge, or filling that has become loose or has fallen out) An infection or an abscessed tooth Significant bleeding from the oral tissues Trauma to the oral tissues causing discomfort or pain Same Day Appointments for Dental Emergencies! Appointments Whatever the dental emergency is, we will always make every effort to see you and treat you as soon as possible. No injury is too big or too small! We keep appointment times available for emergency cases so that you are able to access a dentist and get seen as quickly as possible, even if you are not a regular patient of ours. We recognize that the pain and stress involved in dealing with a dental emergency can be extreme, and we will always do our best to ensure that you are relaxed, calm, and comfortable during your visit. If you think you require emergency treatment, call us immediately to schedule your appointment today! In dental emergency situations, Dolphin Dental is here for you! If you think you might require emergency dental treatment, or you have any questions about a dental issue or emergency dental treatment generally, call us immediately at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to provide you with the care you need. Book Now We look forward to hearing from you soon! Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up your Emergency Dentistry appointment today! Hygiene Healthy teeth and gums are the cornerstone of a healthy mouth and a beautiful smile! That is why Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer dental hygiene and teeth cleaning appointments, to help you achieve the optimal oral health you desire. Regular home care, while important, focuses on areas of the teeth above the gum line (called scaling). A professional dental cleaning can not only clean your teeth above the gum line, but below the gum line as well (subgingival scaling and root planing). It is only through regular scaling and root planing that tartar, plaque, and bacteria can be removed from hard-to-reach areas below the gum line that home care cannot reach. Regular professional cleanings can help keep your teeth and gums healthy from top to bottom! Regular Hygiene and Teeth Cleanings Help Maintain Optimal Oral Health! What Happens at a Dental Hygiene and Teeth Cleaning Appointment? Appointment A complete periodontal assessment A complete check of your gum tissue, checking for any gum recession, the presence of gingivitis, and other possible gum disease. An intra-oral exam to check the gum tissue, tongue, and lips for confirmation of health Scaling Scaling is a process of removing plaque, tartar (calculus) and bacteria from your teeth so your gums and bone that make up the foundation of your teeth remain healthy and disease free. Polishing , to remove stains from your teeth. Fluoride treatment (if chosen). After your dental cleaning, you will be provided with an option to receive fluoride treatment. Fluoride is a natural mineral that helps strengthen the enamel (outer layer of your teeth) and prevent cavities. An oral cancer screening At each visit we make our best efforts to screen your oral tissues (including the head, neck, and jaw area) for confirmation of health and signs of oral cancer. The goal is to identify mouth cancer in the early stages or even before it turns into cancer, when there is a better chance for treatment and cure. Digital x-rays , when required. Radiography helps us detect cavities in between teeth, assess bone levels, and detect other problems of the oral cavity. Your dental surgeon will decide what type of images you need and how often you need them based on your oral health. Research shows that radiation received from digital x-ray machines is less than the radiation you receive from natural background sources. At Dolphin Dental, we make sure we follow the ALARA (as low as reasonably achievable) policy. Sealants (if chosen) Sealants are protective coatings that are applied on deep grooves of back teeth to prevent cavity formation in the future. Sealant application is a quick, easy, and painless procedure. How Often Should You Visit Us for an Oral Hygiene and Check Up Visit? Cleaning Dolphin Dental understands that each patient will require a different hygiene and checkup schedule. Most people come in for a dental hygiene appointment every 6 months, although some people may benefit from coming in every 3-4 months, while others may be able to visit every 9-12 months. Genetics, home care, grinding habits, and teeth positioning are all key factors. For those patients experiencing gum disease, heavy staining, loose teeth, or heavy calculus buildup, a higher frequency of cleaning will help keep teeth healthier. We will discuss with you how often you should visit us for a dental cleaning/checkup based on your specific and individual needs. Dolphin Dental is committed to helping you and your family on the road to optimal oral health. If you have any questions about your dental hygiene, or you would like to set up a regular scaling/teeth cleaning and/or checkup, call us at (416) 429-3317 and our qualified and experienced dental hygienists will make sure you are taken care of! Root Canal If you think you might require a root canal, Dolphin Dental is here for you! A root canal treatment can save your natural teeth from extraction and prevent the need for further intervention down the road. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer root canal therapy so you can achieve optimal oral health and wellness. What is Root Canal Therapy? Process Root canal therapy (RCT) is needed when the nerve of a tooth is affected by decay or infection. The most common reasons that a tooth becomes compromised is because of a crack or fracture, a deep cavity, or an injury to the tooth. In order to save the tooth from extraction, the pulp (the living tissue inside the tooth), nerves, bacteria, and any decay are removed, and the resulting space is filled with special, medicated dental materials which restores the tooth to its full function. An injured tooth that is left untreated can lead to extreme pain, a dental abscess, or possible tooth loss. RCT is the treatment of choice to save a tooth that otherwise would die and have to be removed. Patients often believe that removing a problematic tooth is the only solution, but that is not always the case. Extracting (or pulling) a tooth may often be more costly and can cause significant problems for adjacent teeth. Root canal treatment is highly successful and usually lasts a lifetime, although on occasion, a tooth may have to be re-treated due to new infections. If you are experiencing any tooth pain and think you might benefit from a root canal, or you have any questions or concerns about the root canal procedure, contact Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you! Clear If you are looking for an effective orthodontic treatment option to straighten teeth, deal with spaces between your teeth, or address a bite that requires correction, Clear Aligners might be right for you! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer this virtually invisible solution to help you achieve the healthy, straight, and beautiful smile you desire. What are Clear Aligners? Aligners Clear aligners, sometimes referred to as invisible aligners, are clear, plastic, custom made aligners that correct crooked or misaligned teeth. An alternative to older, more visible and/or fixed orthodontic treatments like metal braces, they are virtually invisible and conveniently removable. They are made from special transparent plastic/synthetic material and are custom-designed for each patient to ensure proper fit and a final result that will be a smile that truly fits you! They can be used to treat a variety of dental issues, including crowded teeth, overbite, diastema/spacing, underbite, open bite, and misaligned primary (baby) teeth. What is Involved in Clear Aligners Treatment? Treatment Process At Dolphin Dental, our qualified team will conduct a thorough examination of your mouth and teeth alignment, which will include a digital scan of your mouth, and then provide you with a recommendation. If a clear aligner system is recommended, a custom treatment plan will be designed just for you. After design and fabrication of the clear aligners using digital 3D technology, you will see your dentist every few weeks in order to check your progress and change to the next set of Aligners in your series. Each aligner moves (realigns) the teeth by a small amount, so multiple sets will be required to slowly move your teeth into the correct position according to your individual treatment plan. Depending on the patient, treatment can take anywhere from six to twenty-four months, sometimes longer. After treatment is complete, a custom clear retainer is made from a mold of the newly straightened teeth. Retainers should be worn every night while sleeping to ensure malocclusion does not recur over time. Dolphin Dental will monitor the alignment of your teeth continually, during your regularly scheduled patient visits, and make recommendations if necessary based on the specifics of your case. Straight teeth are healthy teeth! If you think you might benefit from clear aligners and would like to set up a consultation, or you have any questions about clear aligners, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to help! Book Now We look forward to hearing from you soon! Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up your Clear Aligners appointment today! Content: TMJ/TMD | Dolphin Dental | East York Toronto Dentist | 416-429-3317 (416) 429-3317 Book Now (416) 429-3317 dolphingenie@rogers.com Why Choose Dolphin Dental Dental Insurance & Finances Dental Appointment & Office Policies FAQs Health & Safety Services Family Dentistry Children’s Dentistry Happy Visits Cavity Free Club Fillings and Extractions Sports Mouthguards Early Intervention Orthodontics Emergency Dentistry Dental Hygiene & Teeth Cleanings Root Canal Therapy Clear Aligners Orthodontics TMJ/TMD Therapy Bruxism Grinding Appliances Clear Aligners Cosmetic Dentistry Teeth Whitening Dental Crowns Dental Bridges Porcelain Veneers Cosmetic Tooth Bonding Dental Implants White Fillings Porcelain Inlays & Onlays Oral Surgery Tooth Extractions Wisdom Teeth Extractions Dental Implants Periodontal Care Gum Disease Oral Health Laser Dental Treatment New Patients Team Dr. Priya Rao Dental Assistant Team Dental Hygienists Team Dental Administration Team Contact Book Now TMJ/TMD Therapy East York Dentist Your East York Choice for TMD/TMJ Treatment! TMD/TMJ If you suffer from constant headaches or neck pain, have trouble opening and closing your mouth when speaking and eating, have noticed that your jaw clicks or pops, and/or have been experiencing radiating pain in your jaw, you might be suffering from TMJ pain, otherwise known as Temporomandibular Dysfunction (TMD). Dolphin Dental is here to help! We are pleased to offer TMJ/TMD treatment options to help ease your pain and discomfort, and help you attain better health and wellness. What is TMJ? TMJ The temporomandibular joint, or TMJ, is the joint that connects your lower jaw to your skull on both sides of your head and allows for the opening and closing of your mouth, as well as moving your jaw from side to side. Generally, and for many people, the TMJ works well and causes no problems. Other times, and for some people, problems arise with the TMJ, which can cause extreme pain and affect your overall health. What is TMD? TMD Temporomandibular Disorders (TMD) are problems associated with the movement of the jaw, and pain in and around the jaw. For some people, the temporomandibular joint (TMJ) becomes stressed and overworked. When this happens, it can lead to TMD. Bruxism, which presents as grinding or clenching of the teeth, is one of the most common forms of TMD. Symptoms of TMD Symptoms Difficulty or pain opening your mouth. Your jaw may even lock, preventing any movement at all Head, neck, face, or shoulder discomfort Ear pain or hearing difficulties (this can include ringing ears) Teeth grinding or clenching Constant fatigue Popping or grating sounds in the jaw joints Constant headaches or migraines Treatment for TMD Treatment Because there is such a variety of symptoms associated with TMD, discovering the right treatment can be complicated and can involve multiple health care professionals including physiotherapists, chiropractors, massage therapists etc. With proper diagnosis, Dolphin Dental may be able to determine the root cause of your problem and work with you to come up with a customized treatment plan for your specific needs. The ultimate goal is to help relieve the pain and discomfort and address any damage associated with your TMD. Dolphin Dental is here to help you deal with your TMJ/TMD so you can get back to pain-free living! If you are experiencing jaw pain, coupled with any other symptoms of TMD, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to help! Book Now We look forward to hearing from you soon! Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up your TMJ/TMD appointment today! Bruxism Grinding Appliances are worn over your upper or lower teeth to realign your jaw and help ease the pain associated with any misalignment. The idea is that by realigning the jaw and preventing the jaw from clicking, it will help alleviate symptoms. The appliance also helps to protect teeth from physical wear and tear involved in the constant teeth grinding of bruxism, so that instead of wearing down the enamel of your teeth, you bite against the appliance. Bruxism grinding appliances are custom made to fit your unique mouth and will be specially constructed to take into account the severity of your condition; the more you grind, the harder and more sturdy the appliance may be. Cosmetic Dolphin Dentistry is pleased to offer a wide range of cosmetic dentistry options to meet all your cosmetic needs! From whitening stained or yellow teeth, to repairing crooked or misshapen teeth, to treating malformed or incorrect bites and dealing with simple injuries, Dolphin Dental looks forward to helping you achieve the smile of your dreams! What is Cosmetic Dentistry? Dentistry Cosmetic Dentistry describes any dental procedure that is intended to improve the appearance of your smile (including teeth, gums, and/or bite) by addressing things like colour, shape, size, position, gaps, alignment, or the overall appearance of your smile. The procedures involved may not necessarily address the health or functionality of your smile. Cosmetic dentistry is usually performed for aesthetic reasons. While dentists are always concerned with your overall dental health and having a cosmetic procedure done MAY improve your dental health, the procedure is focused on how your mouth will look, rather than how well it functions. Whitening Dolphin Dental understands the importance of aesthetics and appearance; we all want a bright and white smile! Unfortunately, things like coffee, tea, red wine, berries, cola, smoking, and general aging can cause staining, yellowing, and general discolouration. With our in-office and take-home teeth whitening, we can help you achieve the bright white smile you have always wanted. Smile With Confidence With Our East York Dentist Teeth Whitening Service! In-Office Teeth Whitening In-Office In-office teeth whitening is performed by a dentist at our clinic. Your dentist will first cover your lips and gums, leaving only your teeth exposed. A hydrogen peroxide gel will be applied to your teeth, and then exposed to a special LED light that activates the gel. The light works to break apart the carbon bonds that create the stains and discolouration, thereby starting the bleaching process, without affecting the structure of your teeth in any way. When the process is complete, you will be left with whiter and brighter teeth. The process typically takes about 60 minutes, and is repeated 3-4 times for best results. Take-Home Teeth Whitening Take-Home Take-home teeth whitening offers you a safe and effective way to whiten your teeth at your own convenience, in the privacy of your own home. We send you home with custom made plastic trays that we create using impressions of your teeth, along with a hydrogen peroxide whitening gel. The trays are filled with the gel and worn over teeth for approximately 30 minutes, twice a day. Most patients see excellent results in just two weeks, although individual results can vary. Whichever method you choose, you can expect Dolphin Dental’s teeth whitening services to remove most stains and discolouration quickly, effectively, and safely, so you can achieve the white and bright smile of your dreams. Professional teeth whitening is a safe, easy, and effective way to achieve a brighter and whiter smile. If you would like to learn more or you would like to book a teeth whitening consultation with our Dolphin Dental team, please do not hesitate to contact us (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to help. Dental If you are looking for a way to restore the function and overall aesthetics of discoloured or damaged teeth, dental crowns might be right for you! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer this cosmetic dental option so you can achieve the smile you desire! What is a Dental Crown? Crowns Dental crowns, or caps as they are often referred to, are common dental restorations that cover, or fully ‘cap’, damaged teeth to improve the appearance and health of your teeth. Whether from disease, decay, an accident, wear and tear, stains, or damage, dental crowns can help restore your smile to what it once was. Even extreme damage that seems beyond repair may be corrected with a dental crown. Crowns are made using a variety of materials, including gold alloy, porcelain, zirconia or a mixture of these. Dolphin Dental will work closely with you to choose the appropriate crown for your situation. The main difference between a crown and other dental restorations like fillings or inlays and onlays, is that a crown covers the entire tooth that is visible above the gum line and becomes the new outer surface of your tooth. Dental crowns are ideal for teeth with damage, decay, large existing restorations, or teeth that have been treated with root canal therapy. Benefits of a Dental Crown Benefits Replaces missing teeth (as part of a bridge) Enhances the aesthetics of your smile by correcting staining, cracks, or tooth decay Reduces space between teeth and makes teeth more functional Optimizes alignment between teeth Provides support to badly broken or misplaced teeth Fixes biting and chewing problems by making teeth stronger and therefore more functional A reliable solution for major dental problems caused from accidents or wear and tear A long-term solution for a wide variety of aesthetic concerns – with proper care, they can last 20-30 years. If you are interested in learning more about dental crowns, or you would like to discuss whether dental crowns might be right for you, please do not hesitate to contact us (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to help! Content: Dental Bridges | Dolphin Dental | East York Toronto Dentist | 416-429-3317 (416) 429-3317 Book Now (416) 429-3317 dolphingenie@rogers.com Why Choose Dolphin Dental Dental Insurance & Finances Dental Appointment & Office Policies FAQs Health & Safety Services Family Dentistry Children’s Dentistry Happy Visits Cavity Free Club Fillings and Extractions Sports Mouthguards Early Intervention Orthodontics Emergency Dentistry Dental Hygiene & Teeth Cleanings Root Canal Therapy Clear Aligners Orthodontics TMJ/TMD Therapy Bruxism Grinding Appliances Clear Aligners Cosmetic Dentistry Teeth Whitening Dental Crowns Dental Bridges Porcelain Veneers Cosmetic Tooth Bonding Dental Implants White Fillings Porcelain Inlays & Onlays Oral Surgery Tooth Extractions Wisdom Teeth Extractions Dental Implants Periodontal Care Gum Disease Oral Health Laser Dental Treatment New Patients Team Dr. Priya Rao Dental Assistant Team Dental Hygienists Team Dental Administration Team Contact Book Now Dental Bridges East York Dentist Your East York Choice for Dental Bridges! Dental If you are interested in a solution for one or more missing teeth, a dental bridge might be right for you! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer this very natural looking restoration option that can replace one or more missing teeth and give you the smile you have always wanted! What is a Dental Bridge? Bridge A dental bridge, also known as a fixed partial denture, is a restoration option that is used to replace one tooth, or multiple teeth in the same area. Using abutment teeth to anchor the bridge to, a dental bridge essentially ‘bridges’ or fills in the gap that is left behind from a missing tooth, by placing a false tooth in the area that the gap is. Dental bridges are shaped and coloured just like your natural teeth, so they seamlessly blend in with the rest of your mouth. Adjacent teeth will need to be slightly modified and will be crowned so that the bridge remains in place and your overall bite is stabilized. The end result will be a strong, durable, and aesthetically pleasing solution for missing teeth that can offer your smile back to its original state. If your confidence has been affected because of one or more missing teeth, a dental bridge might be the solution for you. If you would like to learn more about dental bridges, or you are wondering whether you would be a good candidate for a dental bridge, please do not hesitate to contact us (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to help! Porcelain If you are looking for a long-lasting solution for cracks, gaps, chips or discolouration in your front teeth, porcelain veneers might be right for you! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer porcelain veneers to help you achieve the smile you have always wanted. What is a Porcelain Veneer? Veneers A porcelain veneer is made up of thin layers of porcelain that bond directly to the front surface of your teeth in order to protect chipped, damaged, or discoloured teeth, or improve the overall aesthetics of teeth. Porcelain veneers are a simple and versatile option for improving your smile and are incredibly durable; with proper care they can last up to 15 years. Tooth Bonding If you are looking for an effective way to improve the look of a discoloured, chipped, or cracked tooth, dental bonding might be right for you! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer dental bonding, so you can achieve the smile you have always wanted. What is Dental Bonding? How? Dental bonding is an effective cosmetic dental procedure that repairs a decayed, chipped, worn, fractured, or discoloured tooth. A durable tooth-coloured plastic resin is applied to the affected tooth, and then hardened with a special LED light that works to ‘bond’ the material securely to the tooth. Once completed, dental bonding can improve or restore a person’s smile to what it once was. How Does Dental Bonding Work? Benefits Dental bonding is a simple and effective procedure that begins with your dentist first cleaning the area where the resin will be applied. Next, a resin that closely matches your natural tooth colour is applied layer by layer to the affected tooth and then molded to the shape of your tooth. The resin is then hardened with a special LED light. Once hardened, any required corrections are made to ensure that the tooth looks correct. The final step in the process involves polishing the tooth. It is important to note that resin can stain, and is most susceptible to staining within the first few hours following treatment. Consequently, it is important to avoid smoking, as well as drinking things like coffee, tea, or red wine immediately after your procedure. If you have a chipped or cracked tooth, discolouration, or a gap you are interested in correcting, dental bonding might be right for you! If you have any questions about dental bonding, or you would like to set up a consultation to see if dental bonding might be right for you, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 225-1991 and we will be happy to help! Book Now We look forward to hearing from you soon! Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up your Cosmetic Tooth Bonding appointment today! Dental If you are looking for an effective solution for one or more missing teeth, dental implants might be right for you! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer the convenience of dental implants as a foundation for replacement teeth that feel, look, and function just like your natural teeth. What is a Dental Implant? Implant A dental implant is a small, metal, screw-like titanium post that is permanently placed in your jawbone where missing teeth are, to replace tooth roots. It is fixed into your jaw, bonds to your bone, and creates a very strong foundation on which to mount artificial replacement teeth. Your artificial teeth will look and function much like real ones. Dental implant surgery can offer a welcome alternative to dentures or bridgework that does not fit well and can offer an option for those who lack the natural tooth roots to allow building dentures or bridgework. Dental Implant Process Process How dental implant surgery is performed depends on the type of implant and the condition of your jawbone. Dental implant surgery may involve several procedures. The major benefit of implants is solid support for your new teeth – a process that requires the bone to heal tightly around the implant. At Dolphin Dental, our experienced surgeons have been providing patients with implants for decades and have advanced training and certifications in implant dentistry. We use only the highest quality materials and improved technology for implant placement. Benefits of Dental Implants Benefits Natural appearance of tooth Preserves facial structure Preserves surrounding structure of teeth Allows you the comfort and confidence to eat, speak, laugh, and smile Reliable and high functioning Durable and long-lasting Easy to care for Eliminates the embarrassment or inconvenience caused when removing dentures Helps prevent cavities; since implants are cavity proof, your smile is no longer as vulnerable to tooth decay Dolphin Dental understands the importance of replacing missing teeth with a natural looking and high functioning restoration. Dental implants can help you achieve your goal of a beautiful, healthy smile. If you would like to learn more about dental implants, or you would like to make an appointment to see if you are a candidate for dental implants, please do not hesitate to contact us (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to help! Book Now We look forward to hearing from you soon! Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up your Dental Implants appointment today! Fillings If you have tooth decay or damage that requires treatment, Dolphin Dental is here for you! Decay or damage is usually seen in the form of a cavity, which cannot be ignored, or it can worsen and/or potentially lead to a root canal treatment or extraction. Cavities are most often treated with a filling. White filings are an ideal option to restore the function and shape of teeth, because they seamlessly blend in with the rest of your teeth so no one will know you even have a filling. Let Dolphin Dental help you restore your damaged or decayed teeth with white fillings! What is a White Filling? Fillings A cavity is an area of the tooth that has decayed and formed a hole. Cavities should be filled by a dentist as soon as possible, or they can grow in size and worsen, and eventually cause unnecessary discomfort, pain, root canal or extraction. Fillings can be used on chipped or worn-down teeth as well, Filling material can be white or have a metallic finish. White fillings, also known as tooth coloured or composite fillings, are an aesthetically pleasing choice since the composite resin material they are made up of is colour matched to seamlessly blend in with the rest of your tooth enamel, while also offering the strength and durability you would expect from a filling. Dolphin Dental is committed to helping you achieve optimal oral health. If you believe you may have a cavity that requires a filling, or you have any questions or concerns about white fillings or the white filling process, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to help! Content: Porcelain Inlays & Onlays | Dolphin Dental | East York Toronto Dentist (416) 429-3317 Book Now (416) 429-3317 dolphingenie@rogers.com Why Choose Dolphin Dental Dental Insurance & Finances Dental Appointment & Office Policies FAQs Health & Safety Services Family Dentistry Children’s Dentistry Happy Visits Cavity Free Club Fillings and Extractions Sports Mouthguards Early Intervention Orthodontics Emergency Dentistry Dental Hygiene & Teeth Cleanings Root Canal Therapy Clear Aligners Orthodontics TMJ/TMD Therapy Bruxism Grinding Appliances Clear Aligners Cosmetic Dentistry Teeth Whitening Dental Crowns Dental Bridges Porcelain Veneers Cosmetic Tooth Bonding Dental Implants White Fillings Porcelain Inlays & Onlays Oral Surgery Tooth Extractions Wisdom Teeth Extractions Dental Implants Periodontal Care Gum Disease Oral Health Laser Dental Treatment New Patients Team Dr. Priya Rao Dental Assistant Team Dental Hygienists Team Dental Administration Team Contact Book Now Porcelain Inlays & Onlays East York Dentist Your East York Choice for Porcelain Inlays & Onlays! Inlays If your tooth is too damaged to support a filling but is not so damaged that it requires a crown, an inlay or onlay might be right for you. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer this effective restorative option that allows your teeth to keep their function and natural look! What is an Inlay and Onlay? Onlays Inlays and Onlays fill in gaps in teeth when a filling will not work because the tooth is too damaged to support it, and a crown would be too invasive. An inlay fills in cavities and hollows between the cusps, mainly covering the chewing surface of your tooth. An onlay is a more substantial reconstruction, doing more than just filling in cavities on the chewing surface; it also extends out and covers one or more cusps of the tooth. Both are similar to crowns in that they are made from the same material and serve the same function. The difference is that, unlike a crown, they do not cover the entire surface of the tooth. Both inlays and onlays are made of porcelain, gold, or composite resin. In recent years porcelain has been increasingly popular as the material of choice because of its strength and colour, which can potentially match the colour of your natural teeth. Benefits of Inlays and Onlays Benefits Made from high quality material Durable and long lasting with proper care Can treat tooth decay while also preserving tooth structure Can eliminate tooth sensitivity Can give the restored tooth a natural and aesthetically pleasing appearance If you think you might benefit from an inlay or onlay, or you have any questions about inlays or onlays, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to help! Book Now We look forward to hearing from you soon! Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up your Porcelain Inlays & Onlays appointment today! Extraction While adult teeth are meant to last a lifetime, their removal is sometimes recommended or necessary. Dolphin Dental is pleased to be able to provide safe, painless and effective tooth extractions when recommended by your dentist. Why might a Tooth Need to be Removed? Why? While tooth extraction is always a last resort, it may be the best treatment option in certain situations. Severe tooth decay, advanced periodontal disease, or fractures that cannot be repaired are all situations that might call for the removal of a tooth. Some teeth require extraction in advance of orthodontic treatment, or because they are positioned poorly in the mouth. The Tooth Extraction Process Process There is no need to worry about pain! Your dentist will first administer local anesthetic to numb the tooth, jawbone, gums and the surrounding area. You will remain completely pain-free and comfortable throughout the procedure, although you may feel some slight pressure during the process. After the tooth is removed, it is not uncommon to experience some mild discomfort immediately after the freezing wears off. Ibuprofen or acetaminophen are recommended at this time. Any bleeding and swelling is usually quite minimal. Your dentist will go over with you exactly what to expect. If you think you might require tooth extractions, or you have any questions about the tooth extraction process, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to help! Extraction Although extraction is always a last resort, there are circumstances where it is the best course of action. Wisdom teeth extractions is a common procedure, performed regularly. If your wisdom teeth are causing you any problems, Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer safe, effective, and painless wisdom teeth extractions! What are Wisdom Teeth? Wisdom Teeth Located in the very back of the mouth, wisdom teeth are the last and final set of molars to appear, usually between the ages of 14-30. Some people never get their wisdom teeth. For many people, wisdom teeth come in properly and cause no issues. For many others however, wisdom teeth can be problematic, and dental intervention is necessary in order to avoid more complications later on. If left untreated, problematic wisdom teeth can lead to gum disease, tooth decay, or occlusion problems, all of which can cause extreme pain and discomfort. Why Might Wisdom Teeth Need to Be Removed? Why? Oftentimes, there is not enough room in the mouth to accommodate the wisdom teeth, which can prevent them from growing in properly. This can result in considerable pain, infection, and chronic headaches. For some, wisdom teeth emerge only partially through the gums, which can result in cavities, gum infection and/or extreme pain. If wisdom teeth grow in an unusual direction, the uneven development can cause complications, including  damage to adjacent molars. The more common reason for removal is when there is not enough room for molars to grow in. This is called ‘Impacted’ wisdom teeth. When teeth are impacted, the area around can become a fertile ground for bacteria to grow, which can lead to gum infection, which can ultimately cause a great deal of pain, discomfort, swelling, and illness. Often, it will be recommended that wisdom teeth be removed before they erupt, in order to avoid future problems and costly surgical procedures. How Do I Know if My Wisdom Teeth Are Coming In? Process Sensitive areas of swelling in the back of the mouth Frequent headaches that did not occur previously Pain in the jaw Having your wisdom teeth removed is not as scary as it seems! Like with any dental procedure, with the right anesthetic, the appropriate tools, and gentle hands, the process is painless and straightforward. If you have been experiencing any pain, swelling, or discomfort, or you have any questions or concerns about your wisdom teeth or the wisdom teeth removal process, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to help! Periodontal If you notice swollen, red, bleeding gums, and/or any loose teeth, you might be suffering from periodontal disease. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer periodontal care and a variety of periodontal disease treatment options for patients who suffer from gum disease and want to manage the disease and assorted symptoms. What is Periodontal Care? What? Periodontal Care focuses on caring for the gums and surrounding tissue inside of the mouth. Periodontal disease attacks the gums and bone that support teeth. Plaque is a sticky film of food debris, bacteria, and saliva. If plaque is not removed, it turns into calculus (tartar). When plaque and calculus are not removed, they begin to destroy the gums and bone. Periodontal disease is characterized by red, swollen and bleeding gums. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer a wide variety of periodontal services to meet all your needs. Treatment recommendations are conservative, and we limit surgery to when it is absolutely necessary. In particularly complex cases, we may refer patients to a specialist. Periodontal Services Services Early stages of periodontal disease are best treated with nonsurgical therapy. Even in severe cases of periodontal disease, there are nonsurgical therapies that we recommend prior to surgery. If you have any questions about periodontal care, or you think you might require periodontal services, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and will be happy to help! Content: Gum Disease | Dolphin Dental | East York Toronto Dentist | 416-429-3317 (416) 429-3317 Book Now (416) 429-3317 dolphingenie@rogers.com Why Choose Dolphin Dental Dental Insurance & Finances Dental Appointment & Office Policies FAQs Health & Safety Services Family Dentistry Children’s Dentistry Happy Visits Cavity Free Club Fillings and Extractions Sports Mouthguards Early Intervention Orthodontics Emergency Dentistry Dental Hygiene & Teeth Cleanings Root Canal Therapy Clear Aligners Orthodontics TMJ/TMD Therapy Bruxism Grinding Appliances Clear Aligners Cosmetic Dentistry Teeth Whitening Dental Crowns Dental Bridges Porcelain Veneers Cosmetic Tooth Bonding Dental Implants White Fillings Porcelain Inlays & Onlays Oral Surgery Tooth Extractions Wisdom Teeth Extractions Dental Implants Periodontal Care Gum Disease Oral Health Laser Dental Treatment New Patients Team Dr. Priya Rao Dental Assistant Team Dental Hygienists Team Dental Administration Team Contact Book Now Gum Disease East York Dentist Your East York Choice for Gum Disease Treatment! Gum Disease Periodontal (gum) disease affects about 30% of the adult population and is the leading cause of tooth loss in adults. Many denture cases begin because of this chronic condition. Although not curable, with a dedicated professional hygiene regimen and consistent at-home care, it is controllable. Gum disease can advance with few signs or symptoms in the early stages. Many patients diagnosed with this condition experience no pain and are surprised by the quiet yet swift damage that periodontal disease leaves in its wake. The gums and bones surrounding teeth provide teeth with structural support, without which, even strong and healthy teeth will become endangered. Regular dental exams, professional cleanings, and good oral hygiene practices at home are essential to detecting and strategically managing periodontal/gum disease. Gum disease (or poor gum health) is associated with a number of serious health conditions – refer to the section on “Oral Health & Overall Health” below – and while the underlying or causal mechanisms are not yet fully understood, experts are unanimous in their view that a healthy mouth and a regimen to keep it that way is a good thing. What Causes Gum Disease? Causes Our mouths provide a home to millions of bacteria, both beneficial and harmful. Bacterial waste forms a sticky substance, called plaque, which adheres to teeth. Brushing and flossing aim to remove plaque before it mineralizes into tartar. Tartar becomes a colony for more bacteria releasing toxins into the gums. Gums react to this bacterial invasion with an inflammatory response thanks to your immune system. Around the base of each tooth, there is a small collar of gum tissue that forms a small crevice or pocket. This warm, dark environment provides a perfect habitat for deeper tartar and bacteria to infiltrate. Early inflammation results in bleeding gums, known as gingivitis. Bacteria left untreated and undisturbed successfully create a chronic infection in the periodontal pocket. In many cases, the bone begins to deteriorate around the teeth. While gums may be slightly tender at this stage, there is generally minimal discomfort as the bone begins to erode. More than 50% of the bone around your teeth can disappear before any signs of looseness or pain appear. The bone around teeth may never regenerate, so this loss may become permanent and harder to control as the bacteria penetrate deeper into the gums. Untreated gum disease leads to abscesses and generalized tooth loss in many advanced cases. Diagnosis of Gum Disease Diagnosis There are several factors to consider before making a gum disease diagnosis. The small collar of gum, or pocket, around each tooth usually sits 2-3 millimeters deep. The Dolphin Dental team can measure and chart multiple areas using a small measuring device called a periodontal probe to detect periodontal disease. In addition, manual inspection of the shape and texture of your gums, and digital x-rays to analyze the bones in the jaw, all help to provide us with a comprehensive picture of the health of your gums. Treatment of Gum Disease Treatment After establishing a diagnosis and defining the severity of gum disease, we can develop a personalized treatment plan. Milder forms with little or no bone loss can be managed with one or two visits with our hygiene team, which may bring the condition under control. When you leave our office with a strategy for daily home care and an established schedule for maintenance, little additional treatment may be needed. If the inflammation has advanced and measurable bone loss is evident, a proactive approach to stop further deterioration should be strongly considered. Often, we will suggest gentle numbing of your gums, and a more in-depth cleaning process sometimes called root planing or deep scaling. Over a few visits, a portion of your mouth at a time will be deep cleaned. The infected pocket around each tooth, including the mineralized tartar, must be carefully cleaned out with hand and ultrasonic instruments. Dr. Rao and her team will also provide you with other specific strategies to help you with your home care routine, as gum disease can be controlled. Dedicated daily efforts must be consistent to control the disease. Home Care for Gum Disease Home Care Regular home care is critical to arrest the progression of gum disease. Within a few hours of cleaning, the bacteria begin to repopulate and adhere to the teeth. Plaque left undisturbed will start to harden and mineralize within a day. Routine home care must involve brushing twice a day, flossing once a day, and rinsing your mouth with water after every meal. Since gum pockets previously damaged by bacteria can be difficult to reach at home, a regular maintenance schedule with your dentist and hygienist is essential. Dolphin Dental can customize your plan to include 2, 3 or 4 visits a year depending on the severity of disease, its response to treatment, and the consistency of your home care. If our combined efforts do not slow or stop the progression of your gum disease, we will refer you to a specialist, known as a periodontist. With specialized training in many gum conditions, they will be able to recommend further treatment. If you think you may be suffering from gum disease and would like to set up an appointment, or you have any questions or concerns about gum disease or the diagnosis and/or treatment process, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to help! Book Now We look forward to hearing from you soon! Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up your Gum Disease appointment today! Oral Health Research continues to establish clear links between bacterial disease in your mouth and ailments in other parts of the body. Studies show a link between oral bacteria and conditions such as heart disease, stroke, arthritis, Alzheimer’s, and even certain types of cancers. The relationship between a person’s oral health and their whole-body health has never been more understood than it is today. Bleeding gums provide a direct pathway into the bloodstream, a journey that oral bacteria can quickly take. If an open wound existed on your skin, infection would be a concern. Gum tissue that bleeds should be looked at no differently. This helps explain why researchers continue to identify oral bacteria deposits in various areas of our bodies. Diabetes and other auto-immune disorders lower the body’s ability to fight infection, allowing uncontrolled gum disease to advance faster and with more destruction. Research also confirms that the inflammation in the mouth can aggravate diabetes, making it harder to control. This two-way relationship between two chronic conditions emphasizes the importance of optimal oral health . Dolphin Dental encourages patients to take an active role in their oral health, in order to take care of their overall health! With dedication to education, maintenance, and prevention, Dolphin Dental can help you achieve and maintain optimal oral health. We look forward to hearing from you soon! Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up your Oral Health appointment today! Laser Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer dental laser treatment to remove infected gum tissue and help you achieve optimal oral health. This innovative technology is a minimally invasive option when facing gum surgery, cavity treatment, or other oral issues. What is Laser Dental Treatment? What? All lasers work by delivering energy in the form of extremely focused light beams. When lasers are used for surgical and dental procedures, the lasers serve as a cutting instrument or a vaporizer of tissue that it comes in contact with, and they are used to alter or remove tissue in small amounts. When used during teeth-whitening treatment, the lasers act as a heat source and enhance the effect of tooth-bleaching agents. Dentists use lasers in a variety of situations involving the inside of the mouth, to remove overgrown tissue, reshape gums, or whiten teeth. What Can Laser Dentistry Treat? Treatment Canker sore and cold sore pain treatments Root canal infections Gum disease Removing gum inflammation Gum reshaping Biopsies Exposing wisdom teeth Regenerating damaged nerves Removing benign oral tumors Benefits of Laser Dental Treatment Benefits Preserves healthy tissues, since only those tissues affected by gum disease are removed Reduces patient pain and discomfort Allows gum and bone tissue to grow back Patients are less likely to require sutures Anesthesia may not be necessary The laser will sterilize the gums, making infection less likely Less damage to gums shortens healing time Patients lose less blood than with traditional surgery We look forward to hearing from you soon! Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up your Laser Dental Treatment appointment today! No Referral Necessary! If you are looking for a dentist for you and your entire family, consider Dolphin Dental! We are pleased to offer a wide range of dental services to meet all your oral health needs and we welcome all new patients. We are committed to providing you and your family with the highest-quality dental care possible, in a caring, relaxed, and comfortable environment. Your First Visit to Dolphin Dental At Dolphin Dental, we want to ensure that your first visit with us is as pleasant as possible. Upon entering our clinic, you will be immediately greeted by our Administrative Team, who will do their very best to make you feel welcome and comfortable. Your appointment time will be a dedicated one-on-one time with your Dolphin Dental Team, who will spend as much time as necessary to discuss all your dental health needs and goals. If you cannot remember the last time you went to the dentist, let Dolphin Dental show you how EASY and COMFORTABLE it can be! During your visit with us, we will make sure that you clearly understand what is going on in your mouth, using pictures and videos if necessary. All options will be thoroughly explained to you, and any questions you have will be answered. By using technology such as X-Rays, we can image your entire mouth in just seconds, which will help us understand your oral health and how we may help improve or maintain it. We will never pressure you to proceed with any procedure unless you are totally comfortable and completely understand the need for it. New Patient Online Forms At Dolphin Dental, we want to save you time. That is why we have online forms that you can download right from our website. This allows you to print them off and fill them in at your convenience, in the privacy of your own home. At Dolphin Dental, we always try to keep your dental visit as efficient as possible, ensuring that it starts and ends on time. We always follow up every visit so that you can provide us with any feedback on how we can further improve to meet ALL of your needs. Our goal is always to keep you aware of your oral health needs. To accomplish this, we keep in touch with our patients via whatever technology they are most comfortable with, making sure it fits within your schedule. This helps you stay informed and attain all your dental health goals. New Patient Forms We look forward to hearing from you soon!
