Content: Privacy Policy | Dolphin Dental | East York Toronto Dentist | 416-429-3317 (416) 429-3317 Book Now (416) 429-3317 dolphingenie@rogers.com Why Choose Dolphin Dental Dental Insurance & Finances Dental Appointment & Office Policies FAQs Health & Safety Services Family Dentistry Children’s Dentistry Happy Visits Cavity Free Club Fillings and Extractions Sports Mouthguards Early Intervention Orthodontics Emergency Dentistry Dental Hygiene & Teeth Cleanings Root Canal Therapy Clear Aligners Orthodontics TMJ/TMD Therapy Bruxism Grinding Appliances Clear Aligners Cosmetic Dentistry Teeth Whitening Dental Crowns Dental Bridges Porcelain Veneers Cosmetic Tooth Bonding Dental Implants White Fillings Porcelain Inlays & Onlays Oral Surgery Tooth Extractions Wisdom Teeth Extractions Dental Implants Periodontal Care Gum Disease Oral Health Laser Dental Treatment New Patients Team Dr. Priya Rao Dental Assistant Team Dental Hygienists Team Dental Administration Team Contact Book Now Our Privacy Policy Dentist Our Website & Online Privacy Policy At Dolphin Dental, we respect your privacy. That is why… Dolphin Dental (from now on the “Site”) is for your personal education, information, communication, and entertainment. Please feel free to browse the Site. You may download material displayed on the Site for non-commercial, personal use only, provided you also retain all copyright and other proprietary notices contained on the materials. You may not, however, distribute, modify, transmit, reuse, repost or use the content of the Site for public or commercial purposes, including the text, images, audio, and video, without Dolphin Dental’s written permission. Your access to and use of the Site is also subject to the following Terms and Conditions and all applicable laws. By accessing and browsing the Site, you accept, without limitation or qualification, the Terms and Conditions and acknowledge that any other agreements between you and Dolphin Dental are superseded and of no force or effect. We may collect the following information: Name and job title Contact information, including email address Demographic information such as postal code, preferences, and interests Other information relevant to customer surveys and/or offers We require this information to better understand your needs and provide you with a better service, and in particular for the following reasons: Internal record keeping. We may use the information to improve our products and services. We may periodically send promotional email about new products, special offers or other information which we think you may find interesting, using the email address you have provided us. From time to time, we may use your information to contact you for market research purposes. We may contact you by email, phone, or mail. We may use the information to customize the website according to your interests. We may provide your information to our third-party partners for marketing or promotional purposes. We will never sell your information. Security We are committed to ensuring that your information is secure. To prevent unauthorized access or disclosure, we have put in place suitable physical, electronic, and managerial procedures to safeguard and secure the information we collect online. How we use cookies A cookie is a small file which asks permission to be placed on your computer’s hard drive. Once you agree, the file is added, and the cookie helps analyze web traffic or lets you know when you visit a particular site. Cookies allow web applications to respond to you as an individual. The web application can tailor its operations to your needs, likes, and dislikes by gathering and remembering information about your preferences. We use traffic log cookies to identify which pages are being used. This helps us analyze data about web page traffic and improve our website to tailor it to customer needs. We only use this information for statistical analysis purposes, and then the data is removed from the system. Overall, cookies help us provide you with a better website by enabling us to monitor which pages you find useful and which you do not. A cookie in no way gives us access to your computer or any information about you other than the data you choose to share with us. You can choose to accept or decline cookies. Most web browsers automatically accept cookies, but you can usually modify your browser setting to decline cookies if you prefer. This may prevent you from taking full advantage of the website. Links to other websites Our website may contain links to enable you to visit other websites of interest easily. However, once you have used these links to leave our Site, you should note that we do not have any control over that other website. Therefore, we cannot be responsible for the protection and privacy of any information you provide while visiting such sites. This privacy statement does not govern such sites. You should exercise caution and look at the privacy statement applicable to the website in question. Controlling your personal information You may choose to restrict the collection or use of your personal information in the following ways: Whenever you are asked to fill in a form on the website, look for the box that you can click to indicate that you do not want the information to be used by anybody for direct marketing purposes If you have previously agreed to allow us to use your personal information for direct marketing purposes, you may change your mind at any time by writing to or emailing us at dolphingenie@rogers.com We will not sell, distribute, or lease your personal information to third parties unless we have your permission or are required by law. We may use your personal information to send you promotional information about third parties, which we think you may find interesting if you tell us that you wish this to happen. You may request details of personal information which we hold about you under the Data Protection Act 1998. A small fee will be payable. If you would like a copy of the information held on you, please write to dolphingenie@rogers.com If you believe that any information, we are holding on you is incorrect or incomplete, please write to or email us as soon as possible at the above address. We will promptly correct any information found to be incorrect. If you have any questions about any of the above, please do not hesitate to contact us for more clarification! Revised: April 18, 2022. We look forward to hearing from you soon. Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up an appointment today! A strong believer in lifelong learning, Dr. Rao keeps herself updated in the science and practice of dentistry through various continuing education courses and programs. She has also completed a mini-residency program in Implant Dentistry from TIDE, Canada. Dr. Rao is passionate about dentistry and enjoys treating patients of all ages, including boisterous 3-year-olds and the youthful 90-year-olds! In her words, “The best part of my dental practice is the look and radiance on my patient’s face after I have taken care of their pain or dental problems”. Dr. Rao lives in East York, Toronto, and when she is not busy tending to her patients, enjoys painting, reading, gardening, and exploring new places and countries. Root Canal If you think you might require a root canal, Dolphin Dental is here for you! A root canal treatment can save your natural teeth from extraction and prevent the need for further intervention down the road. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer root canal therapy so you can achieve optimal oral health and wellness. What is Root Canal Therapy? Process Root canal therapy (RCT) is needed when the nerve of a tooth is affected by decay or infection. The most common reasons that a tooth becomes compromised is because of a crack or fracture, a deep cavity, or an injury to the tooth. In order to save the tooth from extraction, the pulp (the living tissue inside the tooth), nerves, bacteria, and any decay are removed, and the resulting space is filled with special, medicated dental materials which restores the tooth to its full function. An injured tooth that is left untreated can lead to extreme pain, a dental abscess, or possible tooth loss. RCT is the treatment of choice to save a tooth that otherwise would die and have to be removed. Patients often believe that removing a problematic tooth is the only solution, but that is not always the case. Extracting (or pulling) a tooth may often be more costly and can cause significant problems for adjacent teeth. Root canal treatment is highly successful and usually lasts a lifetime, although on occasion, a tooth may have to be re-treated due to new infections. If you are experiencing any tooth pain and think you might benefit from a root canal, or you have any questions or concerns about the root canal procedure, contact Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you! Book Now We look forward to hearing from you soon! Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up your Root Canal Therapy appointment today! Clear If you are looking for an effective orthodontic treatment option to straighten teeth, deal with spaces between your teeth, or address a bite that requires correction, Clear Aligners might be right for you! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer this virtually invisible solution to help you achieve the healthy, straight, and beautiful smile you desire. What are Clear Aligners? Aligners Clear aligners, sometimes referred to as invisible aligners, are clear, plastic, custom made aligners that correct crooked or misaligned teeth. An alternative to older, more visible and/or fixed orthodontic treatments like metal braces, they are virtually invisible and conveniently removable. They are made from special transparent plastic/synthetic material and are custom-designed for each patient to ensure proper fit and a final result that will be a smile that truly fits you! They can be used to treat a variety of dental issues, including crowded teeth, overbite, diastema/spacing, underbite, open bite, and misaligned primary (baby) teeth. What is Involved in Clear Aligners Treatment? Treatment Process At Dolphin Dental, our qualified team will conduct a thorough examination of your mouth and teeth alignment, which will include a digital scan of your mouth, and then provide you with a recommendation. If a clear aligner system is recommended, a custom treatment plan will be designed just for you. After design and fabrication of the clear aligners using digital 3D technology, you will see your dentist every few weeks in order to check your progress and change to the next set of Aligners in your series. Each aligner moves (realigns) the teeth by a small amount, so multiple sets will be required to slowly move your teeth into the correct position according to your individual treatment plan. Depending on the patient, treatment can take anywhere from six to twenty-four months, sometimes longer. After treatment is complete, a custom clear retainer is made from a mold of the newly straightened teeth. Retainers should be worn every night while sleeping to ensure malocclusion does not recur over time. Dolphin Dental will monitor the alignment of your teeth continually, during your regularly scheduled patient visits, and make recommendations if necessary based on the specifics of your case. Straight teeth are healthy teeth! If you think you might benefit from clear aligners and would like to set up a consultation, or you have any questions about clear aligners, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to help! Book Now We look forward to hearing from you soon! Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up your Clear Aligners appointment today! Cosmetic Dolphin Dentistry is pleased to offer a wide range of cosmetic dentistry options to meet all your cosmetic needs! From whitening stained or yellow teeth, to repairing crooked or misshapen teeth, to treating malformed or incorrect bites and dealing with simple injuries, Dolphin Dental looks forward to helping you achieve the smile of your dreams! What is Cosmetic Dentistry? Dentistry Cosmetic Dentistry describes any dental procedure that is intended to improve the appearance of your smile (including teeth, gums, and/or bite) by addressing things like colour, shape, size, position, gaps, alignment, or the overall appearance of your smile. The procedures involved may not necessarily address the health or functionality of your smile. Cosmetic dentistry is usually performed for aesthetic reasons. While dentists are always concerned with your overall dental health and having a cosmetic procedure done MAY improve your dental health, the procedure is focused on how your mouth will look, rather than how well it functions. Whitening Dolphin Dental understands the importance of aesthetics and appearance; we all want a bright and white smile! Unfortunately, things like coffee, tea, red wine, berries, cola, smoking, and general aging can cause staining, yellowing, and general discolouration. With our in-office and take-home teeth whitening, we can help you achieve the bright white smile you have always wanted. Smile With Confidence With Our East York Dentist Teeth Whitening Service! In-Office Teeth Whitening In-Office In-office teeth whitening is performed by a dentist at our clinic. Your dentist will first cover your lips and gums, leaving only your teeth exposed. A hydrogen peroxide gel will be applied to your teeth, and then exposed to a special LED light that activates the gel. The light works to break apart the carbon bonds that create the stains and discolouration, thereby starting the bleaching process, without affecting the structure of your teeth in any way. When the process is complete, you will be left with whiter and brighter teeth. The process typically takes about 60 minutes, and is repeated 3-4 times for best results. Take-Home Teeth Whitening Take-Home Take-home teeth whitening offers you a safe and effective way to whiten your teeth at your own convenience, in the privacy of your own home. We send you home with custom made plastic trays that we create using impressions of your teeth, along with a hydrogen peroxide whitening gel. The trays are filled with the gel and worn over teeth for approximately 30 minutes, twice a day. Most patients see excellent results in just two weeks, although individual results can vary. Whichever method you choose, you can expect Dolphin Dental’s teeth whitening services to remove most stains and discolouration quickly, effectively, and safely, so you can achieve the white and bright smile of your dreams. Professional teeth whitening is a safe, easy, and effective way to achieve a brighter and whiter smile. If you would like to learn more or you would like to book a teeth whitening consultation with our Dolphin Dental team, please do not hesitate to contact us (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to help. Periodontal If you notice swollen, red, bleeding gums, and/or any loose teeth, you might be suffering from periodontal disease. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer periodontal care and a variety of periodontal disease treatment options for patients who suffer from gum disease and want to manage the disease and assorted symptoms. What is Periodontal Care? What? Periodontal Care focuses on caring for the gums and surrounding tissue inside of the mouth. Periodontal disease attacks the gums and bone that support teeth. Plaque is a sticky film of food debris, bacteria, and saliva. If plaque is not removed, it turns into calculus (tartar). When plaque and calculus are not removed, they begin to destroy the gums and bone. Periodontal disease is characterized by red, swollen and bleeding gums. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer a wide variety of periodontal services to meet all your needs. Treatment recommendations are conservative, and we limit surgery to when it is absolutely necessary. In particularly complex cases, we may refer patients to a specialist. Periodontal Services Services Early stages of periodontal disease are best treated with nonsurgical therapy. Even in severe cases of periodontal disease, there are nonsurgical therapies that we recommend prior to surgery. If you have any questions about periodontal care, or you think you might require periodontal services, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and will be happy to help! Laser Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer dental laser treatment to remove infected gum tissue and help you achieve optimal oral health. This innovative technology is a minimally invasive option when facing gum surgery, cavity treatment, or other oral issues. What is Laser Dental Treatment? What? All lasers work by delivering energy in the form of extremely focused light beams. When lasers are used for surgical and dental procedures, the lasers serve as a cutting instrument or a vaporizer of tissue that it comes in contact with, and they are used to alter or remove tissue in small amounts. When used during teeth-whitening treatment, the lasers act as a heat source and enhance the effect of tooth-bleaching agents. Dentists use lasers in a variety of situations involving the inside of the mouth, to remove overgrown tissue, reshape gums, or whiten teeth. What Can Laser Dentistry Treat? Treatment Canker sore and cold sore pain treatments Root canal infections Gum disease Removing gum inflammation Gum reshaping Biopsies Exposing wisdom teeth Regenerating damaged nerves Removing benign oral tumors Benefits of Laser Dental Treatment Benefits Preserves healthy tissues, since only those tissues affected by gum disease are removed Reduces patient pain and discomfort Allows gum and bone tissue to grow back Patients are less likely to require sutures Anesthesia may not be necessary The laser will sterilize the gums, making infection less likely Less damage to gums shortens healing time Patients lose less blood than with traditional surgery We look forward to hearing from you soon! Children's Dolphin Dental is proud to offer services to patients of ALL ages. We are pleased to offer Children’s Dentistry services tailored specifically to children and their unique needs, from birth all the way to adolescence. Dolphin Dental believes in the importance of creating a positive experience at the dentist early on, in order to encourage a lifetime of good oral care. As parents ourselves, we understand the unique concerns and fears that children often have. With our family-friendly atmosphere, and our caring and always-smiling team members, we are here to make sure your child’s visit to the dentist is a happy one, each and every time. Our goal with pediatric visits is to ensure that your child is always comfortable and relaxed, while also setting the foundation they can draw from for the rest of their life. We hope your child leaves eager and enthusiastic to continue on with their future dental visits! When should I bring my child to the dentist for the first time? Dentistry The Canadian Dental Association recommends that children obtain a dental examination within 6 months of the eruption of their first tooth, or by the age of one, whichever comes first. It is important to see children early on, and review important aspects of dental care, health, and diet. Happy Visits Happy Visits Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer complimentary Happy Visits to all children under the age of 3. We aim to ensure these visits are fun, and that children feel safe and relaxed throughout. Our goal is to introduce your child to the dental visit experience and allow them to become familiar with the entire process, while ensuring it is enjoyable. These visits help ensure that your child has a positive association with the dentist and oral health in general, which will set the stage for a lifetime of good oral health. Cavity Free Club Cavity Free This is a club your kids will want to be a part of! Our cavity-free club acts as a reward system to help our youngest patients learn and maintain good oral hygiene habits. Every young patient may become a member; all they have to do is take care of their teeth by brushing and flossing daily, and if they come to their appointment and have no cavities, they become a member! Once they become a member, they will be entered into a draw to receive a monthly prize. They will also receive a small toy which they can choose from our cavity-free club reward chest! Fillings and Extractions Fillings If your child has a damaged or cracked tooth in need of repair, we may recommend a filling, which will help prevent bacteria from entering the crack or damaged area of the tooth. Fillings in children are just as necessary as they are for adults, because untreated cavities can cause discomfort and pain, and cavities can lead to other problems including infection. Extractions may also be necessary, depending on the health of a tooth, whether there is any overcrowding, or in preparation for orthodontic treatment later on. Our dentists will discuss with you any recommendations regarding fillings and extractions for your child. Rest assured that should your child require a filling or an extraction, they will remain pain-free, comfortable, and relaxed throughout the entire procedure. For more complicated procedures your child may be referred to a specialist. Sports Mouthguards Sports If your child has a damaged or cracked tooth in need of repair, we may recommend a filling, which will help prevent bacteria from entering the crack or damaged area of the tooth. Fillings in children are just as necessary as they are for adults, because untreated cavities can cause discomfort and pain, and cavities can lead to other problems including infection. Extractions may also be necessary, depending on the health of a tooth, whether there is any overcrowding, or in preparation for orthodontic treatment later on. Our dentists will discuss with you any recommendations regarding fillings and extractions for your child. Rest assured that should your child require a filling or an extraction, they will remain pain-free, comfortable, and relaxed throughout the entire procedure. For more complicated procedures your child may be referred to a specialist. Early Intervention Orthodontics Orthodontics Early intervention orthodontics is orthodontic treatment for children starting around the age of 7. Intervening early on can reduce the need for tooth extraction and jaw surgery later on, correct certain problems before they appear, encourage better facial development, shorten the length of time of any orthodontic treatment needed later on, and provide patients with a better overall result in the end. Traditional orthodontic treatment begins after most or all of a patient’s adult teeth have grown in. However, certain issues with dental alignment, bite, and facial development can begin to appear long before the last few adult teeth appear. By correcting any of these problems early on, future orthodontic treatment can be faster and easier, and sometimes even unnecessary! It is important to note that not all orthodontic problems can be solved with early intervention, which is why it is important that your child have an initial consultation with their dentist as soon as possible after they turn seven. Dolphin Dental is committed to ensuring children get an early start on their oral journey so that their teeth, gums, and smile are healthy from day one. We are pleased to provide dental care to children of any age, and we take special care to ensure our youngest patients always feel comfortable and safe. If you have any questions about the oral health needs of your child, or you would like to set up a visit for your child, call us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to help! Emergency At Dolphin Dental, we understand that emergencies sometimes happen! We have seen it all, and we know the importance of dealing with emergency dental issues as soon as possible. If you are unsure whether something is an emergency or not, we offer this advice; if it hurts, it is an emergency! This is because even injuries that seem small or superficial can still affect the living tissue inside of the tooth. When a dental emergency arises, Dolphin Dental is here to help make you smile again. What Constitutes an Emergency? Dentistry Sudden and severe pain that will not go away Swelling and fever A loose tooth A broken, chipped, or cracked tooth A tooth knocked out of its socket Fillings that are causing discomfort or pain, or any dental device malfunction (a retainer, bridge, or filling that has become loose or has fallen out) An infection or an abscessed tooth Significant bleeding from the oral tissues Trauma to the oral tissues causing discomfort or pain Same Day Appointments for Dental Emergencies! Appointments Whatever the dental emergency is, we will always make every effort to see you and treat you as soon as possible. No injury is too big or too small! We keep appointment times available for emergency cases so that you are able to access a dentist and get seen as quickly as possible, even if you are not a regular patient of ours. We recognize that the pain and stress involved in dealing with a dental emergency can be extreme, and we will always do our best to ensure that you are relaxed, calm, and comfortable during your visit. If you think you require emergency treatment, call us immediately to schedule your appointment today! In dental emergency situations, Dolphin Dental is here for you! If you think you might require emergency dental treatment, or you have any questions about a dental issue or emergency dental treatment generally, call us immediately at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to provide you with the care you need. Hygiene Healthy teeth and gums are the cornerstone of a healthy mouth and a beautiful smile! That is why Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer dental hygiene and teeth cleaning appointments, to help you achieve the optimal oral health you desire. Regular home care, while important, focuses on areas of the teeth above the gum line (called scaling). A professional dental cleaning can not only clean your teeth above the gum line, but below the gum line as well (subgingival scaling and root planing). It is only through regular scaling and root planing that tartar, plaque, and bacteria can be removed from hard-to-reach areas below the gum line that home care cannot reach. Regular professional cleanings can help keep your teeth and gums healthy from top to bottom! Regular Hygiene and Teeth Cleanings Help Maintain Optimal Oral Health! What Happens at a Dental Hygiene and Teeth Cleaning Appointment? Appointment A complete periodontal assessment A complete check of your gum tissue, checking for any gum recession, the presence of gingivitis, and other possible gum disease. An intra-oral exam to check the gum tissue, tongue, and lips for confirmation of health Scaling Scaling is a process of removing plaque, tartar (calculus) and bacteria from your teeth so your gums and bone that make up the foundation of your teeth remain healthy and disease free. Polishing , to remove stains from your teeth. Fluoride treatment (if chosen). After your dental cleaning, you will be provided with an option to receive fluoride treatment. Fluoride is a natural mineral that helps strengthen the enamel (outer layer of your teeth) and prevent cavities. An oral cancer screening At each visit we make our best efforts to screen your oral tissues (including the head, neck, and jaw area) for confirmation of health and signs of oral cancer. The goal is to identify mouth cancer in the early stages or even before it turns into cancer, when there is a better chance for treatment and cure. Digital x-rays , when required. Radiography helps us detect cavities in between teeth, assess bone levels, and detect other problems of the oral cavity. Your dental surgeon will decide what type of images you need and how often you need them based on your oral health. Research shows that radiation received from digital x-ray machines is less than the radiation you receive from natural background sources. At Dolphin Dental, we make sure we follow the ALARA (as low as reasonably achievable) policy. Sealants (if chosen) Sealants are protective coatings that are applied on deep grooves of back teeth to prevent cavity formation in the future. Sealant application is a quick, easy, and painless procedure. How Often Should You Visit Us for an Oral Hygiene and Check Up Visit? Cleaning Dolphin Dental understands that each patient will require a different hygiene and checkup schedule. Most people come in for a dental hygiene appointment every 6 months, although some people may benefit from coming in every 3-4 months, while others may be able to visit every 9-12 months. Genetics, home care, grinding habits, and teeth positioning are all key factors. For those patients experiencing gum disease, heavy staining, loose teeth, or heavy calculus buildup, a higher frequency of cleaning will help keep teeth healthier. We will discuss with you how often you should visit us for a dental cleaning/checkup based on your specific and individual needs. Dolphin Dental is committed to helping you and your family on the road to optimal oral health. If you have any questions about your dental hygiene, or you would like to set up a regular scaling/teeth cleaning and/or checkup, call us at (416) 429-3317 and our qualified and experienced dental hygienists will make sure you are taken care of! That is why… Dolphin Dental (from now on the “Site”) is for your personal education, information, communication, and entertainment. Please feel free to browse the Site. You may download material displayed on the Site for non-commercial, personal use only, provided you also retain all copyright and other proprietary notices contained on the materials. You may not, however, distribute, modify, transmit, reuse, repost or use the content of the Site for public or commercial purposes, including the text, images, audio, and video, without Dolphin Dental’s written permission. Your access to and use of the Site is also subject to the following Terms and Conditions and all applicable laws. By accessing and browsing the Site, you accept, without limitation or qualification, the Terms and Conditions and acknowledge that any other agreements between you and Dolphin Dental are superseded and of no force or effect. We may collect the following information: Name and job title Contact information, including email address Demographic information such as postal code, preferences, and interests Other information relevant to customer surveys and/or offers We require this information to better understand your needs and provide you with a better service, and in particular for the following reasons: Internal record keeping. We may use the information to improve our products and services. We may periodically send promotional email about new products, special offers or other information which we think you may find interesting, using the email address you have provided us. From time to time, we may use your information to contact you for market research purposes. We may contact you by email, phone, or mail. We may use the information to customize the website according to your interests. We may provide your information to our third-party partners for marketing or promotional purposes. We will never sell your information. Security We are committed to ensuring that your information is secure. To prevent unauthorized access or disclosure, we have put in place suitable physical, electronic, and managerial procedures to safeguard and secure the information we collect online. How we use cookies A cookie is a small file which asks permission to be placed on your computer’s hard drive. Once you agree, the file is added, and the cookie helps analyze web traffic or lets you know when you visit a particular site. Cookies allow web applications to respond to you as an individual. The web application can tailor its operations to your needs, likes, and dislikes by gathering and remembering information about your preferences. We use traffic log cookies to identify which pages are being used. This helps us analyze data about web page traffic and improve our website to tailor it to customer needs. We only use this information for statistical analysis purposes, and then the data is removed from the system. Overall, cookies help us provide you with a better website by enabling us to monitor which pages you find useful and which you do not. A cookie in no way gives us access to your computer or any information about you other than the data you choose to share with us. You can choose to accept or decline cookies. Most web browsers automatically accept cookies, but you can usually modify your browser setting to decline cookies if you prefer. This may prevent you from taking full advantage of the website. Links to other websites Our website may contain links to enable you to visit other websites of interest easily. However, once you have used these links to leave our Site, you should note that we do not have any control over that other website. Therefore, we cannot be responsible for the protection and privacy of any information you provide while visiting such sites. This privacy statement does not govern such sites. You should exercise caution and look at the privacy statement applicable to the website in question. Controlling your personal information You may choose to restrict the collection or use of your personal information in the following ways: Whenever you are asked to fill in a form on the website, look for the box that you can click to indicate that you do not want the information to be used by anybody for direct marketing purposes If you have previously agreed to allow us to use your personal information for direct marketing purposes, you may change your mind at any time by writing to or emailing us at dolphingenie@rogers.com We will not sell, distribute, or lease your personal information to third parties unless we have your permission or are required by law. We may use your personal information to send you promotional information about third parties, which we think you may find interesting if you tell us that you wish this to happen. You may request details of personal information which we hold about you under the Data Protection Act 1998. A small fee will be payable. Content: FAQs | Dolphin Dental | East York Toronto Family Dentist | 416-429-3317 (416) 429-3317 Book Now (416) 429-3317 dolphingenie@rogers.com Why Choose Dolphin Dental Dental Insurance & Finances Dental Appointment & Office Policies FAQs Health & Safety Services Family Dentistry Children’s Dentistry Happy Visits Cavity Free Club Fillings and Extractions Sports Mouthguards Early Intervention Orthodontics Emergency Dentistry Dental Hygiene & Teeth Cleanings Root Canal Therapy Clear Aligners Orthodontics TMJ/TMD Therapy Bruxism Grinding Appliances Clear Aligners Cosmetic Dentistry Teeth Whitening Dental Crowns Dental Bridges Porcelain Veneers Cosmetic Tooth Bonding Dental Implants White Fillings Porcelain Inlays & Onlays Oral Surgery Tooth Extractions Wisdom Teeth Extractions Dental Implants Periodontal Care Gum Disease Oral Health Laser Dental Treatment New Patients Team Dr. Priya Rao Dental Assistant Team Dental Hygienists Team Dental Administration Team Contact Book Now Frequently Asked Questions (FAQs) Dentist Have Questions? We Have Answers! FAQs Dolphin Dental is always here to address all your oral health needs. We believe that each and every patient deserves personalized attention and care, with the goal of creating a lifetime of beautiful and healthy smiles. We are often asked questions, and it is always our goal to answer them. Below are some FAQs  (frequently asked questions) to help you learn more about Dolphin Dental. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. Does Dolphin Dental direct bill insurance companies? Yes! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer direct insurance billing , as long as your plan allows it. Do you follow the current Ontario Dental Association Fee Guide? Yes. Dolphin Dental follows the recommended Ontario Dental Association Ontario Dental Fee Guide for all procedure codes. Do you offer evening and weekend appointments? Yes. For your convenience, Dolphin Dental is open until 7pm Monday-Friday, and Saturdays 10:00-4:00. When should I bring my child in for their first visit? Dolphin Dental recommends that you bring your child in within 6 months of the eruption of their first tooth, or by the age of one, whichever comes first. Do you have payment plans? At this time, Dolphin Dental does not have payment plans available. However, we will do our best to work around your budget. Do you perform wisdom teeth extractions at your office? Yes. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer wisdom teeth extractions . We will need to first examine and take a panoramic x-ray to determine if you are a good candidate to have them removed here. If we are unable to perform the procedure in office we will refer you to a very caring specialists in the neighbourhood Do you offer teeth whitening? Can I bill it to my insurance? Yes! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer two different teeth whitening options. In-house teeth whitening for faster results, or take-home teeth whitening trays you can do in the privacy and convenience of your own home. Unfortunately, dental insurance does not cover cosmetic bleaching. Do you offer emergency appointments? Absolutely! Dolphin Dental will do everything we can to see you the same day. Please call us at (416) 429-3317 if you are having a dental emergency. Do you offer Clear Aligners? Yes, Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer Clear Aligners at our office. Your dentist will determine if you are a good candidate for this treatment. My teeth feel fine, do I still need to come in for a check-up? Yes. Dolphin Dental recommends that you come in regularly to ensure we prevent or catch common dental problems early on, such as gum disease and tooth decay from forming. I’m pregnant/breastfeeding. Can I still come to my appointment? Yes. Dolphin Dental recommends dental cleanings for pregnant women at 12 and 24 weeks. X-Rays will not be taken unless there is an urgent issue. If you are breastfeeding, please continue to see the dentist/hygienist for your regular preventative care. How often should I come in for a check-up/cleaning? This depends on the condition of your mouth. It could range anywhere from every 3 months to every 9 months. On average, we typically see patients once every 6 months. Your dentist will determine what schedule is best for you, based on your circumstances. What is a dental crown? A dental crown is a covering or ‘cap’ for your damaged tooth. It restores your tooth to its normal shape, size, and function. It is typically recommended for a structurally weak tooth that is at high risk of breaking. Do you do dental implants at your office? Yes. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer dental implants . We will start with a consultation to determine if you are a good candidate. Do Root Canals/Fillings hurt? During your root canal, we will use a local anesthetic to keep you as comfortable as possible during the procedure. Afterwards, some soreness is normal and can be managed using over the counter pain killers/analgesics. Can I get x-rays with metal braces? Yes. It is completely safe to have x-rays taken on your teeth during your active orthodontic treatment. It is imperative to regularly come in with braces as they can be a bit tricky to clean! Can you tell me what my plan covers? As a courtesy, we try our best to verify all codes prior to you coming in to avoid any surprises! Some plans have services available to dental providers to verify your coverage. Unfortunately, some other providers have very strict privacy rules where they will only release this information to the subscriber of the plan, not the dental office. This means it is not always possible for us to verify on your behalf. Why does my insurance plan only cover an exam every 9 months but, my dentist wants me to come every 6? A dentist’s first priority is your health. Your dentist will first present a plan based on your oral health needs, which may or may not be covered by your dental plan. Your dentist can do their best to work within your plan whenever possible. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. We look forward to hearing from you soon. Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up an appointment today! Content: FAQs | Dolphin Dental | East York Toronto Family Dentist | 416-429-3317 (416) 429-3317 Book Now (416) 429-3317 dolphingenie@rogers.com Why Choose Dolphin Dental Dental Insurance & Finances Dental Appointment & Office Policies FAQs Health & Safety Services Family Dentistry Children’s Dentistry Happy Visits Cavity Free Club Fillings and Extractions Sports Mouthguards Early Intervention Orthodontics Emergency Dentistry Dental Hygiene & Teeth Cleanings Root Canal Therapy Clear Aligners Orthodontics TMJ/TMD Therapy Bruxism Grinding Appliances Clear Aligners Cosmetic Dentistry Teeth Whitening Dental Crowns Dental Bridges Porcelain Veneers Cosmetic Tooth Bonding Dental Implants White Fillings Porcelain Inlays & Onlays Oral Surgery Tooth Extractions Wisdom Teeth Extractions Dental Implants Periodontal Care Gum Disease Oral Health Laser Dental Treatment New Patients Team Dr. Priya Rao Dental Assistant Team Dental Hygienists Team Dental Administration Team Contact Book Now Frequently Asked Questions (FAQs) Dentist Have Questions? We Have Answers! FAQs Dolphin Dental is always here to address all your oral health needs. We believe that each and every patient deserves personalized attention and care, with the goal of creating a lifetime of beautiful and healthy smiles. We are often asked questions, and it is always our goal to answer them. Below are some FAQs  (frequently asked questions) to help you learn more about Dolphin Dental. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. Does Dolphin Dental direct bill insurance companies? Yes! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer direct insurance billing , as long as your plan allows it. Do you follow the current Ontario Dental Association Fee Guide? Yes. Dolphin Dental follows the recommended Ontario Dental Association Ontario Dental Fee Guide for all procedure codes. Do you offer evening and weekend appointments? Yes. For your convenience, Dolphin Dental is open until 7pm Monday-Friday, and Saturdays 10:00-4:00. When should I bring my child in for their first visit? Dolphin Dental recommends that you bring your child in within 6 months of the eruption of their first tooth, or by the age of one, whichever comes first. Do you have payment plans? At this time, Dolphin Dental does not have payment plans available. However, we will do our best to work around your budget. Do you perform wisdom teeth extractions at your office? Yes. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer wisdom teeth extractions . We will need to first examine and take a panoramic x-ray to determine if you are a good candidate to have them removed here. If we are unable to perform the procedure in office we will refer you to a very caring specialists in the neighbourhood Do you offer teeth whitening? Can I bill it to my insurance? Yes! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer two different teeth whitening options. In-house teeth whitening for faster results, or take-home teeth whitening trays you can do in the privacy and convenience of your own home. Unfortunately, dental insurance does not cover cosmetic bleaching. Do you offer emergency appointments? Absolutely! Dolphin Dental will do everything we can to see you the same day. Please call us at (416) 429-3317 if you are having a dental emergency. Do you offer Clear Aligners? Yes, Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer Clear Aligners at our office. Your dentist will determine if you are a good candidate for this treatment. My teeth feel fine, do I still need to come in for a check-up? Yes. Dolphin Dental recommends that you come in regularly to ensure we prevent or catch common dental problems early on, such as gum disease and tooth decay from forming. I’m pregnant/breastfeeding. Can I still come to my appointment? Yes. Dolphin Dental recommends dental cleanings for pregnant women at 12 and 24 weeks. X-Rays will not be taken unless there is an urgent issue. If you are breastfeeding, please continue to see the dentist/hygienist for your regular preventative care. How often should I come in for a check-up/cleaning? This depends on the condition of your mouth. It could range anywhere from every 3 months to every 9 months. On average, we typically see patients once every 6 months. Your dentist will determine what schedule is best for you, based on your circumstances. What is a dental crown? A dental crown is a covering or ‘cap’ for your damaged tooth. It restores your tooth to its normal shape, size, and function. It is typically recommended for a structurally weak tooth that is at high risk of breaking. Do you do dental implants at your office? Yes. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer dental implants . We will start with a consultation to determine if you are a good candidate. Do Root Canals/Fillings hurt? During your root canal, we will use a local anesthetic to keep you as comfortable as possible during the procedure. Afterwards, some soreness is normal and can be managed using over the counter pain killers/analgesics. Can I get x-rays with metal braces? Yes. It is completely safe to have x-rays taken on your teeth during your active orthodontic treatment. It is imperative to regularly come in with braces as they can be a bit tricky to clean! Can you tell me what my plan covers? As a courtesy, we try our best to verify all codes prior to you coming in to avoid any surprises! Some plans have services available to dental providers to verify your coverage. Unfortunately, some other providers have very strict privacy rules where they will only release this information to the subscriber of the plan, not the dental office. This means it is not always possible for us to verify on your behalf. Why does my insurance plan only cover an exam every 9 months but, my dentist wants me to come every 6? A dentist’s first priority is your health. Your dentist will first present a plan based on your oral health needs, which may or may not be covered by your dental plan. Your dentist can do their best to work within your plan whenever possible. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. We look forward to hearing from you soon. Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up an appointment today! We Have Answers! FAQs Dolphin Dental is always here to address all your oral health needs. We believe that each and every patient deserves personalized attention and care, with the goal of creating a lifetime of beautiful and healthy smiles. We are often asked questions, and it is always our goal to answer them. Below are some FAQs  (frequently asked questions) to help you learn more about Dolphin Dental. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. Does Dolphin Dental direct bill insurance companies? Yes! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer direct insurance billing , as long as your plan allows it. Do you follow the current Ontario Dental Association Fee Guide? Yes. Dolphin Dental follows the recommended Ontario Dental Association Ontario Dental Fee Guide for all procedure codes. Do you offer evening and weekend appointments? Yes. For your convenience, Dolphin Dental is open until 7pm Monday-Friday, and Saturdays 10:00-4:00. When should I bring my child in for their first visit? Dolphin Dental recommends that you bring your child in within 6 months of the eruption of their first tooth, or by the age of one, whichever comes first. Do you have payment plans? At this time, Dolphin Dental does not have payment plans available. However, we will do our best to work around your budget. Do you perform wisdom teeth extractions at your office? Yes. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer wisdom teeth extractions . We will need to first examine and take a panoramic x-ray to determine if you are a good candidate to have them removed here. If we are unable to perform the procedure in office we will refer you to a very caring specialists in the neighbourhood Do you offer teeth whitening? Can I bill it to my insurance? Yes! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer two different teeth whitening options. In-house teeth whitening for faster results, or take-home teeth whitening trays you can do in the privacy and convenience of your own home. Unfortunately, dental insurance does not cover cosmetic bleaching. Do you offer emergency appointments? Absolutely! Dolphin Dental will do everything we can to see you the same day. Please call us at (416) 429-3317 if you are having a dental emergency. Do you offer Clear Aligners? Yes, Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer Clear Aligners at our office. Your dentist will determine if you are a good candidate for this treatment. My teeth feel fine, do I still need to come in for a check-up? Yes. Dolphin Dental recommends that you come in regularly to ensure we prevent or catch common dental problems early on, such as gum disease and tooth decay from forming. I’m pregnant/breastfeeding. Can I still come to my appointment? Yes. Dolphin Dental recommends dental cleanings for pregnant women at 12 and 24 weeks. X-Rays will not be taken unless there is an urgent issue. If you are breastfeeding, please continue to see the dentist/hygienist for your regular preventative care. How often should I come in for a check-up/cleaning? This depends on the condition of your mouth. It could range anywhere from every 3 months to every 9 months. On average, we typically see patients once every 6 months. Your dentist will determine what schedule is best for you, based on your circumstances. What is a dental crown? A dental crown is a covering or ‘cap’ for your damaged tooth. It restores your tooth to its normal shape, size, and function. It is typically recommended for a structurally weak tooth that is at high risk of breaking. Do you do dental implants at your office? Yes. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer dental implants . We will start with a consultation to determine if you are a good candidate. Do Root Canals/Fillings hurt? During your root canal, we will use a local anesthetic to keep you as comfortable as possible during the procedure. Afterwards, some soreness is normal and can be managed using over the counter pain killers/analgesics. Can I get x-rays with metal braces? Yes. It is completely safe to have x-rays taken on your teeth during your active orthodontic treatment. It is imperative to regularly come in with braces as they can be a bit tricky to clean! Can you tell me what my plan covers? As a courtesy, we try our best to verify all codes prior to you coming in to avoid any surprises! Some plans have services available to dental providers to verify your coverage. Unfortunately, some other providers have very strict privacy rules where they will only release this information to the subscriber of the plan, not the dental office. This means it is not always possible for us to verify on your behalf. Why does my insurance plan only cover an exam every 9 months but, my dentist wants me to come every 6? A dentist’s first priority is your health. Your dentist will first present a plan based on your oral health needs, which may or may not be covered by your dental plan. Your dentist can do their best to work within your plan whenever possible. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. We look forward to hearing from you soon. Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up an appointment today! During your root canal, we will use a local anesthetic to keep you as comfortable as possible during the procedure. Afterwards, some soreness is normal and can be managed using over the counter pain killers/analgesics. Can I get x-rays with metal braces? Yes. It is completely safe to have x-rays taken on your teeth during your active orthodontic treatment. It is imperative to regularly come in with braces as they can be a bit tricky to clean! Can you tell me what my plan covers? As a courtesy, we try our best to verify all codes prior to you coming in to avoid any surprises! Some plans have services available to dental providers to verify your coverage. Unfortunately, some other providers have very strict privacy rules where they will only release this information to the subscriber of the plan, not the dental office. This means it is not always possible for us to verify on your behalf. Why does my insurance plan only cover an exam every 9 months but, my dentist wants me to come every 6? A dentist’s first priority is your health. Your dentist will first present a plan based on your oral health needs, which may or may not be covered by your dental plan. Your dentist can do their best to work within your plan whenever possible. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. We look forward to hearing from you soon. Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up an appointment today! We Have Answers! FAQs Dolphin Dental is always here to address all your oral health needs. We believe that each and every patient deserves personalized attention and care, with the goal of creating a lifetime of beautiful and healthy smiles. We are often asked questions, and it is always our goal to answer them. Below are some FAQs  (frequently asked questions) to help you learn more about Dolphin Dental. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. Does Dolphin Dental direct bill insurance companies? Yes! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer direct insurance billing , as long as your plan allows it. Do you follow the current Ontario Dental Association Fee Guide? Yes. Dolphin Dental follows the recommended Ontario Dental Association Ontario Dental Fee Guide for all procedure codes. Do you offer evening and weekend appointments? Yes. For your convenience, Dolphin Dental is open until 7pm Monday-Friday, and Saturdays 10:00-4:00. When should I bring my child in for their first visit? Dolphin Dental recommends that you bring your child in within 6 months of the eruption of their first tooth, or by the age of one, whichever comes first. Do you have payment plans? At this time, Dolphin Dental does not have payment plans available. However, we will do our best to work around your budget. Do you perform wisdom teeth extractions at your office? Yes. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer wisdom teeth extractions . We will need to first examine and take a panoramic x-ray to determine if you are a good candidate to have them removed here. If we are unable to perform the procedure in office we will refer you to a very caring specialists in the neighbourhood Do you offer teeth whitening? Can I bill it to my insurance? Yes! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer two different teeth whitening options. In-house teeth whitening for faster results, or take-home teeth whitening trays you can do in the privacy and convenience of your own home. Unfortunately, dental insurance does not cover cosmetic bleaching. Do you offer emergency appointments? Absolutely! Dolphin Dental will do everything we can to see you the same day. Please call us at (416) 429-3317 if you are having a dental emergency. Do you offer Clear Aligners? Yes, Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer Clear Aligners at our office. Your dentist will determine if you are a good candidate for this treatment. My teeth feel fine, do I still need to come in for a check-up? Yes. Dolphin Dental recommends that you come in regularly to ensure we prevent or catch common dental problems early on, such as gum disease and tooth decay from forming. I’m pregnant/breastfeeding. Can I still come to my appointment? Yes. Dolphin Dental recommends dental cleanings for pregnant women at 12 and 24 weeks. X-Rays will not be taken unless there is an urgent issue. If you are breastfeeding, please continue to see the dentist/hygienist for your regular preventative care. How often should I come in for a check-up/cleaning? This depends on the condition of your mouth. It could range anywhere from every 3 months to every 9 months. On average, we typically see patients once every 6 months. Your dentist will determine what schedule is best for you, based on your circumstances. What is a dental crown? A dental crown is a covering or ‘cap’ for your damaged tooth. It restores your tooth to its normal shape, size, and function. It is typically recommended for a structurally weak tooth that is at high risk of breaking. Do you do dental implants at your office? Yes. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer dental implants . We will start with a consultation to determine if you are a good candidate. Do Root Canals/Fillings hurt? During your root canal, we will use a local anesthetic to keep you as comfortable as possible during the procedure. Afterwards, some soreness is normal and can be managed using over the counter pain killers/analgesics. Can I get x-rays with metal braces? Yes. It is completely safe to have x-rays taken on your teeth during your active orthodontic treatment. It is imperative to regularly come in with braces as they can be a bit tricky to clean! Can you tell me what my plan covers? As a courtesy, we try our best to verify all codes prior to you coming in to avoid any surprises! Some plans have services available to dental providers to verify your coverage. Unfortunately, some other providers have very strict privacy rules where they will only release this information to the subscriber of the plan, not the dental office. This means it is not always possible for us to verify on your behalf. Why does my insurance plan only cover an exam every 9 months but, my dentist wants me to come every 6? A dentist’s first priority is your health. Your dentist will first present a plan based on your oral health needs, which may or may not be covered by your dental plan. Your dentist can do their best to work within your plan whenever possible. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. We look forward to hearing from you soon. Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up an appointment today! Content: FAQs | Dolphin Dental | East York Toronto Family Dentist | 416-429-3317 (416) 429-3317 Book Now (416) 429-3317 dolphingenie@rogers.com Why Choose Dolphin Dental Dental Insurance & Finances Dental Appointment & Office Policies FAQs Health & Safety Services Family Dentistry Children’s Dentistry Happy Visits Cavity Free Club Fillings and Extractions Sports Mouthguards Early Intervention Orthodontics Emergency Dentistry Dental Hygiene & Teeth Cleanings Root Canal Therapy Clear Aligners Orthodontics TMJ/TMD Therapy Bruxism Grinding Appliances Clear Aligners Cosmetic Dentistry Teeth Whitening Dental Crowns Dental Bridges Porcelain Veneers Cosmetic Tooth Bonding Dental Implants White Fillings Porcelain Inlays & Onlays Oral Surgery Tooth Extractions Wisdom Teeth Extractions Dental Implants Periodontal Care Gum Disease Oral Health Laser Dental Treatment New Patients Team Dr. Priya Rao Dental Assistant Team Dental Hygienists Team Dental Administration Team Contact Book Now Frequently Asked Questions (FAQs) Dentist Have Questions? We Have Answers! FAQs Dolphin Dental is always here to address all your oral health needs. We believe that each and every patient deserves personalized attention and care, with the goal of creating a lifetime of beautiful and healthy smiles. We are often asked questions, and it is always our goal to answer them. Below are some FAQs  (frequently asked questions) to help you learn more about Dolphin Dental. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. Does Dolphin Dental direct bill insurance companies? Yes! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer direct insurance billing , as long as your plan allows it. Do you follow the current Ontario Dental Association Fee Guide? Yes. Dolphin Dental follows the recommended Ontario Dental Association Ontario Dental Fee Guide for all procedure codes. Do you offer evening and weekend appointments? Yes. For your convenience, Dolphin Dental is open until 7pm Monday-Friday, and Saturdays 10:00-4:00. When should I bring my child in for their first visit? Dolphin Dental recommends that you bring your child in within 6 months of the eruption of their first tooth, or by the age of one, whichever comes first. Do you have payment plans? At this time, Dolphin Dental does not have payment plans available. However, we will do our best to work around your budget. Do you perform wisdom teeth extractions at your office? Yes. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer wisdom teeth extractions . We will need to first examine and take a panoramic x-ray to determine if you are a good candidate to have them removed here. If we are unable to perform the procedure in office we will refer you to a very caring specialists in the neighbourhood Do you offer teeth whitening? Can I bill it to my insurance? Yes! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer two different teeth whitening options. In-house teeth whitening for faster results, or take-home teeth whitening trays you can do in the privacy and convenience of your own home. Unfortunately, dental insurance does not cover cosmetic bleaching. Do you offer emergency appointments? Absolutely! Dolphin Dental will do everything we can to see you the same day. Please call us at (416) 429-3317 if you are having a dental emergency. Do you offer Clear Aligners? Yes, Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer Clear Aligners at our office. Your dentist will determine if you are a good candidate for this treatment. My teeth feel fine, do I still need to come in for a check-up? Yes. Dolphin Dental recommends that you come in regularly to ensure we prevent or catch common dental problems early on, such as gum disease and tooth decay from forming. I’m pregnant/breastfeeding. Can I still come to my appointment? Yes. Dolphin Dental recommends dental cleanings for pregnant women at 12 and 24 weeks. X-Rays will not be taken unless there is an urgent issue. If you are breastfeeding, please continue to see the dentist/hygienist for your regular preventative care. How often should I come in for a check-up/cleaning? This depends on the condition of your mouth. It could range anywhere from every 3 months to every 9 months. On average, we typically see patients once every 6 months. Your dentist will determine what schedule is best for you, based on your circumstances. What is a dental crown? A dental crown is a covering or ‘cap’ for your damaged tooth. It restores your tooth to its normal shape, size, and function. It is typically recommended for a structurally weak tooth that is at high risk of breaking. Do you do dental implants at your office? Yes. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer dental implants . We will start with a consultation to determine if you are a good candidate. Do Root Canals/Fillings hurt? During your root canal, we will use a local anesthetic to keep you as comfortable as possible during the procedure. Afterwards, some soreness is normal and can be managed using over the counter pain killers/analgesics. Can I get x-rays with metal braces? Yes. It is completely safe to have x-rays taken on your teeth during your active orthodontic treatment. It is imperative to regularly come in with braces as they can be a bit tricky to clean! Can you tell me what my plan covers? As a courtesy, we try our best to verify all codes prior to you coming in to avoid any surprises! Some plans have services available to dental providers to verify your coverage. Unfortunately, some other providers have very strict privacy rules where they will only release this information to the subscriber of the plan, not the dental office. This means it is not always possible for us to verify on your behalf. Why does my insurance plan only cover an exam every 9 months but, my dentist wants me to come every 6? A dentist’s first priority is your health. Your dentist will first present a plan based on your oral health needs, which may or may not be covered by your dental plan. Your dentist can do their best to work within your plan whenever possible. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. We look forward to hearing from you soon. Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up an appointment today! We Have Answers! FAQs Dolphin Dental is always here to address all your oral health needs. We believe that each and every patient deserves personalized attention and care, with the goal of creating a lifetime of beautiful and healthy smiles. We are often asked questions, and it is always our goal to answer them. Below are some FAQs  (frequently asked questions) to help you learn more about Dolphin Dental. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. Does Dolphin Dental direct bill insurance companies? Yes! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer direct insurance billing , as long as your plan allows it. Do you follow the current Ontario Dental Association Fee Guide? Yes. Dolphin Dental follows the recommended Ontario Dental Association Ontario Dental Fee Guide for all procedure codes. Do you offer evening and weekend appointments? Yes. For your convenience, Dolphin Dental is open until 7pm Monday-Friday, and Saturdays 10:00-4:00. When should I bring my child in for their first visit? Dolphin Dental recommends that you bring your child in within 6 months of the eruption of their first tooth, or by the age of one, whichever comes first. Do you have payment plans? At this time, Dolphin Dental does not have payment plans available. However, we will do our best to work around your budget. Do you perform wisdom teeth extractions at your office? Yes. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer wisdom teeth extractions . We will need to first examine and take a panoramic x-ray to determine if you are a good candidate to have them removed here. If we are unable to perform the procedure in office we will refer you to a very caring specialists in the neighbourhood Do you offer teeth whitening? Can I bill it to my insurance? Yes! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer two different teeth whitening options. In-house teeth whitening for faster results, or take-home teeth whitening trays you can do in the privacy and convenience of your own home. Unfortunately, dental insurance does not cover cosmetic bleaching. Do you offer emergency appointments? Absolutely! Dolphin Dental will do everything we can to see you the same day. Please call us at (416) 429-3317 if you are having a dental emergency. Do you offer Clear Aligners? Yes, Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer Clear Aligners at our office. Your dentist will determine if you are a good candidate for this treatment. My teeth feel fine, do I still need to come in for a check-up? Yes. Dolphin Dental recommends that you come in regularly to ensure we prevent or catch common dental problems early on, such as gum disease and tooth decay from forming. I’m pregnant/breastfeeding. Can I still come to my appointment? Yes. Dolphin Dental recommends dental cleanings for pregnant women at 12 and 24 weeks. X-Rays will not be taken unless there is an urgent issue. If you are breastfeeding, please continue to see the dentist/hygienist for your regular preventative care. How often should I come in for a check-up/cleaning? This depends on the condition of your mouth. It could range anywhere from every 3 months to every 9 months. On average, we typically see patients once every 6 months. Your dentist will determine what schedule is best for you, based on your circumstances. What is a dental crown? A dental crown is a covering or ‘cap’ for your damaged tooth. It restores your tooth to its normal shape, size, and function. It is typically recommended for a structurally weak tooth that is at high risk of breaking. Do you do dental implants at your office? Yes. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer dental implants . We will start with a consultation to determine if you are a good candidate. Do Root Canals/Fillings hurt? During your root canal, we will use a local anesthetic to keep you as comfortable as possible during the procedure. Afterwards, some soreness is normal and can be managed using over the counter pain killers/analgesics. Can I get x-rays with metal braces? Yes. It is completely safe to have x-rays taken on your teeth during your active orthodontic treatment. It is imperative to regularly come in with braces as they can be a bit tricky to clean! Can you tell me what my plan covers? As a courtesy, we try our best to verify all codes prior to you coming in to avoid any surprises! Some plans have services available to dental providers to verify your coverage. Unfortunately, some other providers have very strict privacy rules where they will only release this information to the subscriber of the plan, not the dental office. This means it is not always possible for us to verify on your behalf. Why does my insurance plan only cover an exam every 9 months but, my dentist wants me to come every 6? A dentist’s first priority is your health. Your dentist will first present a plan based on your oral health needs, which may or may not be covered by your dental plan. Your dentist can do their best to work within your plan whenever possible. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. We look forward to hearing from you soon. Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up an appointment today! During your root canal, we will use a local anesthetic to keep you as comfortable as possible during the procedure. Afterwards, some soreness is normal and can be managed using over the counter pain killers/analgesics. Can I get x-rays with metal braces? Yes. It is completely safe to have x-rays taken on your teeth during your active orthodontic treatment. It is imperative to regularly come in with braces as they can be a bit tricky to clean! Can you tell me what my plan covers? As a courtesy, we try our best to verify all codes prior to you coming in to avoid any surprises! Some plans have services available to dental providers to verify your coverage. Unfortunately, some other providers have very strict privacy rules where they will only release this information to the subscriber of the plan, not the dental office. This means it is not always possible for us to verify on your behalf. Why does my insurance plan only cover an exam every 9 months but, my dentist wants me to come every 6? A dentist’s first priority is your health. Your dentist will first present a plan based on your oral health needs, which may or may not be covered by your dental plan. Your dentist can do their best to work within your plan whenever possible. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. We look forward to hearing from you soon. Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up an appointment today! We Have Answers! FAQs Dolphin Dental is always here to address all your oral health needs. We believe that each and every patient deserves personalized attention and care, with the goal of creating a lifetime of beautiful and healthy smiles. We are often asked questions, and it is always our goal to answer them. Below are some FAQs  (frequently asked questions) to help you learn more about Dolphin Dental. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. Does Dolphin Dental direct bill insurance companies? Yes! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer direct insurance billing , as long as your plan allows it. Do you follow the current Ontario Dental Association Fee Guide? Yes. Dolphin Dental follows the recommended Ontario Dental Association Ontario Dental Fee Guide for all procedure codes. Do you offer evening and weekend appointments? Yes. For your convenience, Dolphin Dental is open until 7pm Monday-Friday, and Saturdays 10:00-4:00. When should I bring my child in for their first visit? Dolphin Dental recommends that you bring your child in within 6 months of the eruption of their first tooth, or by the age of one, whichever comes first. Do you have payment plans? At this time, Dolphin Dental does not have payment plans available. However, we will do our best to work around your budget. Do you perform wisdom teeth extractions at your office? Yes. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer wisdom teeth extractions . We will need to first examine and take a panoramic x-ray to determine if you are a good candidate to have them removed here. If we are unable to perform the procedure in office we will refer you to a very caring specialists in the neighbourhood Do you offer teeth whitening? Can I bill it to my insurance? Yes! Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer two different teeth whitening options. In-house teeth whitening for faster results, or take-home teeth whitening trays you can do in the privacy and convenience of your own home. Unfortunately, dental insurance does not cover cosmetic bleaching. Do you offer emergency appointments? Absolutely! Dolphin Dental will do everything we can to see you the same day. Please call us at (416) 429-3317 if you are having a dental emergency. Do you offer Clear Aligners? Yes, Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer Clear Aligners at our office. Your dentist will determine if you are a good candidate for this treatment. My teeth feel fine, do I still need to come in for a check-up? Yes. Dolphin Dental recommends that you come in regularly to ensure we prevent or catch common dental problems early on, such as gum disease and tooth decay from forming. I’m pregnant/breastfeeding. Can I still come to my appointment? Yes. Dolphin Dental recommends dental cleanings for pregnant women at 12 and 24 weeks. X-Rays will not be taken unless there is an urgent issue. If you are breastfeeding, please continue to see the dentist/hygienist for your regular preventative care. How often should I come in for a check-up/cleaning? This depends on the condition of your mouth. It could range anywhere from every 3 months to every 9 months. On average, we typically see patients once every 6 months. Your dentist will determine what schedule is best for you, based on your circumstances. What is a dental crown? A dental crown is a covering or ‘cap’ for your damaged tooth. It restores your tooth to its normal shape, size, and function. It is typically recommended for a structurally weak tooth that is at high risk of breaking. Do you do dental implants at your office? Yes. Dolphin Dental is pleased to offer dental implants . We will start with a consultation to determine if you are a good candidate. Do Root Canals/Fillings hurt? During your root canal, we will use a local anesthetic to keep you as comfortable as possible during the procedure. Afterwards, some soreness is normal and can be managed using over the counter pain killers/analgesics. Can I get x-rays with metal braces? Yes. It is completely safe to have x-rays taken on your teeth during your active orthodontic treatment. It is imperative to regularly come in with braces as they can be a bit tricky to clean! Can you tell me what my plan covers? As a courtesy, we try our best to verify all codes prior to you coming in to avoid any surprises! Some plans have services available to dental providers to verify your coverage. Unfortunately, some other providers have very strict privacy rules where they will only release this information to the subscriber of the plan, not the dental office. This means it is not always possible for us to verify on your behalf. Why does my insurance plan only cover an exam every 9 months but, my dentist wants me to come every 6? A dentist’s first priority is your health. Your dentist will first present a plan based on your oral health needs, which may or may not be covered by your dental plan. Your dentist can do their best to work within your plan whenever possible. If you do not see the answer to your question below, please do not hesitate to contact us at (416) 429-3317 and we will be happy to assist you. We look forward to hearing from you soon. Call Dolphin Dental at (416) 429-3317 to set up an appointment today!
